### [108] [When Rule Violations Are Rare: Chimera Training for Logical Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26171)
*Alejandro Ascarate,Leo Lebrat,Rodrigo Santa Cruz,Clinton Fookes,Olivier Salvado*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对语义约束违规难以通过训练数据捕捉的问题，该论文提出一种神经规则评估器，通过“嵌合体训练”构造特征层面的逻辑反事实样本，在无需真实异常数据的情况下，实现了高精度的语义异常检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多实际异常并非简单的罕见输入，而是对语义约束（如对象共现、动作前提、时空关系）的违规。然而，在训练阶段，这些语义违规的真实样本极其稀少或完全缺失，传统的监督学习方法难以有效捕捉复杂的逻辑关联。

Method: 1. 构建神经规则评估器，将逻辑约束编译为有向无环图（DAG），并利用基于特征的子树MLP门控机制处理逻辑运算。
2. 引入“嵌合体训练（Chimera training）”策略，通过在特征层面对来自不同样本的子树特征进行组合，构造逻辑反事实样本，从而为模型提供充足的监督信号。
3. 利用真值标签对中间逻辑运算符进行监督，结合布尔传播机制学习规则满足概率。

Result: 在CLEVRER、OpenImages和VidOR数据集上的实验表明，该方法在规则级异常检测的AUROC指标上优于传统的独立事件基线和基于同图语义训练的方法，特别是在处理组合式和关系型逻辑约束时表现出显著优势，并能提供具体的异常评分和规则归因。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为神经规则评估器（Neural Rule Evaluator）的新方法，能够有效检测视频和图像中的语义违规。通过引入“嵌合体训练（Chimera training）”机制，该方法在不需要真实异常样本的情况下，通过逻辑反事实推理显著提升了模型对组合式和关系型规则违规的检测能力，并具备良好的可解释性。

Abstract: Many practical anomalies are not merely rare inputs, but violations of semantic constraints: objects co-occur in structured ways, actions imply preconditions, and events satisfy temporal or relational regularities. We study anomaly detection in this setting, where constraints are given as logical rules over learned visual concepts, but real rule violations are rare or absent during training. We propose a neural rule evaluator that compiles each constraint into a directed acyclic graph and learns feature-aware subtree MLP gates for its internal logical operators. Each gate maps child features and edge-level negations to a parent representation and a rule-satisfaction probability, with intermediate supervision obtained from exact Boolean propagation over ground-truth concept labels. The key difficulty is that same-image training data often provide insufficient coverage of informative truth configurations and also allow shortcut solutions. To address this, we introduce chimera training: an operand-level counterfactual construction at the feature level. Instead of mixing input images, we concatenate subtree features from different samples; each operand keeps the hard truth label of the sample it came from, and the chimera target is obtained by applying the node's logical operator to those inherited labels. This supplies supervised logical counterexamples without requiring real anomalous images. Across CLEVRER, OpenImages, and VidOR, the resulting evaluator improves rule-level anomaly AUROC over independent-events and same-image semantic-training baselines, especially for compositional and relational rules. The method yields both scalar anomaly scores and rule-level attributions.

</details>


### [109] [InfoQuant: Shaping Activation Distributions for Low-Bit LLM Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26175)
*Ke Li,Dong An,Xiaoling Zang,Can Ye,Liang Xie,Qibo Qiu,Chen Shen,Xiaofei He,Wenxiao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: InfoQuant 是一种无需训练的量化方法，通过引入峰值抑制正交变换 (PSOT) 将大模型激活值整形为更易于量化的分布，在极低比特（W4A4KV4）下实现了极高的精度保留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型 (LLM) 在低比特激活量化部署时，存在激活值分布与均匀量化器不匹配的问题，表现为激活值中存在离群点且分布不均匀，导致即便进行平滑处理仍会产生巨大量化误差。现有的 PTQ 方法缺乏对“什么样的激活分布更易于离散化”的本质理解。

Method: 提出了 InfoQuant 方法，包含两项核心技术：1. 峰值抑制正交变换 (PSOT)：通过线性变换将激活值调整为更易于量化的分布，使其同时满足数值范围更小和分布更离散的要求；2. 自适应离散点选择：在优化过程中动态选取异常 token，增强了 PSOT 的稳健性。该方法为无需训练 (train-free) 的后训练量化 (PTQ)。

Result: 在多个主流大模型系列上测试表明，InfoQuant 优于现有的 PTQ 及端到端训练基准。在 W4A4KV4（权重、激活、KV Cache 均为 4 比特）的极端配置下，InfoQuant 平均保留了 97% 的 FP16 精度，并将 LLaMA-2 13B 模型的性能差距较此前先进方法缩短了 42%。

Conclusion: InfoQuant 通过将激活值变换重构为面向量化器的分布设计，成功解决了大模型低比特量化中的分布失配问题。该方法证明了优化激活分布的形态（即缩小数值范围并增加离散度）是实现高精度低比特量化的关键，为无需训练的量化技术提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Low-bit activation quantization remains a major bottleneck in efficient large language model (LLM) deployment. The difficulty is not only that activations contain outliers, but that their distributions are often poorly matched to a low-bit uniform quantizer. Existing post-training quantization (PTQ) methods suppress peaks, balance channels, or minimize reconstruction error, yet they rarely specify what activation distribution is actually easy to discretize. As a result, activations may appear numerically smoother while still incurring large quantization error because the quantization range remains wide or most values collapse into a few levels near the mean. We recast activation transformation as quantizer-facing distribution design and analyze quantization error from an information-theoretic perspective. Our analysis shows that quantization-friendly activations should jointly have a smaller numerical range and sufficient dispersion within that range. Guided by this analysis, we propose InfoQuant, a train-free method that employs Peak Suppression Orthogonal Transformation (PSOT) to shape activations into more quantization-friendly distributions. We further introduce adaptive outlier-token selection to improve the robustness of PSOT during optimization. Across multiple LLM families, InfoQuant consistently outperforms prior PTQ and end-to-end training baselines. Under W4A4KV4, it preserves 97% of floating-point accuracy on average and reduces the LLaMA-2 13B performance gap by 42% over the previous state of the art. Code is available at [https://github.com/LLIKKE/InfoQuant](https://github.com/LLIKKE/InfoQuant)

</details>


### [110] [GAC: Noise-Aware Adaptive Mixing for Hybrid SFT-RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26184)
*Yuelin Hu,Zhenbo Yu,Zhengxue Cheng,Wei Liu,Li Song*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了 GAC（噪声感知控制器），通过实时感知训练信号的噪声水平，动态优化监督微调与强化学习的混合权重，显著提升了大型语言模型的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的混合后训练方法通常使用固定的混合策略，无法适应训练过程中监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）信号相对噪声水平随时间变化的特性。

Method: 提出了一种噪声感知控制器（GAC），通过在线估计梯度方差和两种训练信号之间的分歧来动态计算自适应混合权重，并结合了平滑处理、先验指导和有界更新机制。

Result: 在数学、代码、科学和逻辑基准测试中，GAC 相比固定的和基于规则的基准方法表现更优，尤其在大规模模型上效果提升更显著，且训练开销不足 1%。

Abstract: Hybrid post-training usually combines supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, but fixed mixing schedules cannot adapt when the relative noise of the two signals changes over time. The method adds smoothing, prior guidance, and bounded updates while reusing existing training tensors. ### [111] [Max-Window Scale Estimation for Near-Lossless HiF8 W8A8 Quantization-Aware Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26189)
*Yingying Cheng,Jinquan Shi,Li Zhou,Zhiyang He,Zhaoyi Sun,Fan Zhang,Jie Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究分析了LLM进行W8A8量化训练时存在的“amax饱和”和“灾难性遗忘”两种隐蔽故障，并通过改进DTS缩放策略与加入预热阶段，实现了性能几乎无损的量化模型部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低位浮点数（W8A8）量化感知训练（QAT）在部署大型语言模型（LLM）时虽高效，但存在标准训练指标难以察觉的潜在故障模式，特别是延迟张量缩放（DTS）机制引发的问题。本研究旨在系统性识别并解决这些隐蔽的故障，以实现高效且高精度的模型压缩。

Method: 研究人员对OpenPangu-Embedded-1B模型进行了八组受控实验，引入了DTS技术，并提出通过64步历史窗口的保守最大值算法来缓解amax饱和，同时利用500步BF16预热来防止灾难性遗忘。

Result: 通过提出的双重修正策略，量化后的模型在MMLU、HellaSwag和ARC-Challenge基准测试中仅分别下降了0.43%、0.58%和0.22%，训练损失的平均绝对百分比误差（APE）仅为0.11%，验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过采用保守的“最大值算法”延迟张量缩放（DTS）策略并配合BF16预热，可以在低位浮点（W8A8）量化训练中有效解决训练损失无法反映的特定故障模式，从而在实现高效部署的同时几乎不损失模型性能。

Abstract: Quantization-aware training (QAT) with low-bit floating-point formats enables efficient LLM deployment, yet introduces subtle failure modes invisible to standard training metrics. We present a systematic study of HiF8 W8A8 QAT for OpenPangu-Embedded-1B through the lens of Delayed Tensor Scaling (DTS). Across eight controlled experiments, we identify and disentangle two orthogonal failure modes: (i)amax saturation, where delayed scale estimates silently corrupt knowledge-sensitive representations via forward-pass clipping, and (ii)catastrophic forgetting, where an aggressive learning rate overwrites pretrained commonsense knowledge independently of quantization. Neither is detectable from training loss alone. We address amax saturation with a conservative max-algorithm DTS strategy over a 64-step history window, and mitigate forgetting via a 500-step BF16 warmup followed by QAT at lr=10^{-5}. Both fixes are necessary and sufficient: our final configuration achieves 0.43% MMLU drop, 0.58% HellaSwag drop, and 0.22% ARC-Challenge drop versus a matched BF16 baseline, with a training loss APE of only 0.11% over 10,000 steps.

### [112] [Modeling Dynamic Mixtures of Time-Delay Systems from Streaming Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26191)
*Ren Fujiwara,Yasuko Matsubara,Yasushi Sakurai*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理具有输入-输出关系的时序数据流时，难以应对环境突变（状态转换）及输入延迟变化带来的性能衰退，且在维持高精度、鲁棒性与低内存消耗之间存在权衡困难。

Method: 提出了一种基于动态混合时滞系统的在线建模框架，通过马尔可夫参数序列构建总结系统张量，利用张量分解算法从历史信息中提取并选择最匹配当前状态的模型，实现对系统动态和输入延迟的实时捕捉与适应。

Result: 在真实数据集上的实验结果表明，DelayMix在预测精度和适应速度上均优于现有的对比方法，尤其在处理高度非平稳数据时表现出极强的适应性和计算效率。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种名为DelayMix的新型在线建模框架，通过将时序数据流建模为动态混合系统，并结合张量分解技术，有效解决了非平稳时序数据中的环境变化与输入延迟问题，在精度、鲁棒性与内存消耗之间取得了优异平衡。

Abstract: This research addresses the problem of adaptive modeling in time-series data streams with clear input-output relationships. This problem is challenging because rapid system changes (regime shifts) caused by environmental factors or input delay changes degrade model performance, and the trade-off among accuracy, robustness, and memory usage arises when using multiple small models for each time-series pattern. To address these issues, this paper presents an online framework/method that treats streaming time series as dynamic mixtures of time-delay systems. This framework maintains robustness of model tracking and reduces memory usage by summarizing past regimes using a fixed-length representation that captures both the system dynamics and input-output delays. Concretely, this approach constructs a summary system tensor using the system's Markov parameter series, capturing both dynamic behavior and delay characteristics. If necessary, a tensor decomposition algorithm extracts relevant past models from the tensor and helps select the system that best fits the current regime. This method enables rapid adaptation to environmental changes and is computationally efficient. Tests on real datasets show that DelayMix consistently outperforms other methods, achieving superior forecast accuracy and faster adaptation to delays, especially for highly non-stationary data.

### [113] [Co-folding model guided by structural proteomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26192)
*Alon Shtrikman,Nitzan Simchi,Michal Ran Shchory,Sagie Brodsky,Eran Seger,Kirill Pevzner*

TL;DR: AIMS-Fold 是一种新型的生成式人工智能框架，它通过在生成过程中融合 XL-MS 和 HDX-MS 等实验数据，成功解决了蛋白质复合物构象预测难题，为药物研发提供了更精确的工具。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 AIMS-Fold 的推理时引导扩散框架。该框架利用可微物理势能，将交联质谱（XL-MS）的空间约束和氢氘交换质谱（HDX-MS）的溶剂可及性数据集成到预训练的扩散模型采样过程中，从而实时引导蛋白质结构的生成。

Result: AIMS-Fold 通过集成 XL-MS 和 HDX-MS 数据，显著提高了蛋白质复合物的预测准确性。在诱导邻近性靶标的测试中，该方法超越了包括 Boltz-2 在内的最先进的纯计算无引导模型，验证了实验约束与计算模型协同作用的有效性。

Conclusion: AIMS-Fold 证明了将稀疏的实验蛋白质组学数据与扩散模型相结合，能够有效改善蛋白质复合物构象的预测，为诱导邻近药物的结构药物设计提供了一个强有力的计算框架。

Abstract: Protein structure generative models excel at predicting single protein static structures from sequence, but routinely fail to capture the correct conformational state of protein complexes, critical for protein design and induced proximity modalities such as antibodies and PROTACs. While structural proteomics techniques like Cross-Linking Mass Spectrometry (XL-MS) and Hydrogen-Deuterium Exchange (HDX-MS) offer valuable spatial and dynamic insights, integrating these sparse, heterogeneous measurements into these models remains an open challenge. Here, we bridge this gap by combining structural proteomics data with the rich biophysical priors learned by pretrained diffusion models. We introduce AIMS-Fold, an inference-time guided-diffusion framework that actively steers the generative sampling trajectory using differentiable physical potentials derived from XL-MS spatial restraints and HDX-MS solvent accessibility profiles. We demonstrate that these structural methods individually enhance predictive accuracy, and their integration yields synergistic improvement. Crucially, by leveraging these experimental restraints, AIMS-Fold achieves higher accuracy on challenging induced proximity targets than purely computational, unguided state-of-the-art models like Boltz-2. This establishes our framework as a powerful, integrative computational approach for the structure based drug design of induced proximity drugs. Evaluation code will be made publicly available upon publication.

### [114] [Bridging Classification and Reconstruction: Cooperative Time Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26193)
*Qideng Tang,Dai Chaofan,Wubin Ma,Yahui Wu,Haohao Zhou,Tao Zhang,Huan Li,Dalin Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在高质量基准数据集和严格评估协议下的实验表明，CoAD 显著优于现有的深度学习和传统数据挖掘方法。此外，CoAD 具有轻量化和高推理速度的特点，非常适合大规模实时应用场景。

Abstract: Time series anomaly detection (TSAD) has long been a hot research topic in data mining due to its various applications. Recent studies challenge the effectiveness of popular deep learning methods for TSAD, suggesting their failure in detecting subtle and prolonged anomalies. Outlier Exposure (OE) and Masked Autoencoder (MAE) emerge as two promising paradigms (classification and reconstruction) for solving the above problems. However, OE-based methods are constrained by poor generalization, while MAE-based methods are limited by masking misalignment issues. To address these limitations, this paper proposes a novel framework, CoAD, which unifies the two paradigms to leverage their complementary strengths while mitigating their respective weaknesses. In this framework, the classification module generates probability-informed soft masks for the reconstruction module, which in turn alleviates the generalization problem of the classification module. This cooperative design enables CoAD to effectively detect subtle and complex anomalies that are often overlooked by existing methods. Additionally, the classification module is carefully designed to resolve issues related to improper classification granularity and the neglect of frequency information. Extensive experiments on high-quality benchmark datasets, conducted under rigorous evaluation protocols, demonstrate that CoAD significantly outperforms both state-of-the-art deep learning and traditional data mining methods, highlighting the potential of deep learning in TSAD. Moreover, CoAD is lightweight and substantially faster than existing SOTA methods, demonstrating its practical value for large-scale, real-time applications.

### [115] [On the Role of Inductive Bias in Time-Series Pretraining: A Case Study in Learning Generalizable Representations for Clinical Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26194)
*Sharmita Dey,Diego Paez-Granados*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对临床时间序列数据中的小样本和异构性挑战，设计了PathoFM预训练模型，通过融合局部重建与时间动态建模，有效平衡了分类与回归任务的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床时间序列数据通常存在样本量小、异构性高以及协议漂移等挑战，而现有的预训练目标往往难以兼顾分类任务（如病理诊断）和回归任务（如时间预测）。本研究旨在探索哪种归纳偏置能够使模型在不同任务类型和受试者之间实现更好的表示迁移。

Method: 提出了一种以编码器为中心的Transformer架构PathoFM，采用三种互补的预训练目标：1. 局部补全（Local Completion）：重构连续掩码跨度以学习局部结构；2. 时间连续性（Temporal Continuity）：基于观察到的前缀预测中间段，以强制执行平滑性和因果一致性；3. 无监督上下文动力学（Unsupervised In-Context Dynamics）：通过注意力机制利用受试者范例窗口进行条件重构。

Result: 实验对比了分组/对比学习、动力学建模和生成式重构等不同范式，发现动力学中心的混合策略能产生最均衡的迁移效果；分组学习虽增强了判别性但损失了幅度保真度，而纯重构方法保留了波形结构但在分类任务上性能受限。PathoFM结合了局部重构、时间连续性及上下文条件，显著提升了跨受试者的泛化性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种名为PathoFM的预训练框架，通过结合局部重建和时间连续性目标，实现了在分类和回归任务之间表现平衡的通用表示学习，证明了动力学中心混合策略在处理具有异构性和协议漂移的临床时间序列数据中具有优越性。

Abstract: Clinical time-series learning is routinely constrained by small, heterogeneous cohorts and protocol drift, while its downstream use spans both classification (e.g., pathology diagnosis) and regression (e.g., temporal forecasting). These constraints make foundation-model pretraining appealing, but raises an important question of which inductive biases should the pretraining objective impose so that representations transfer across task types and subjects. We study this question in pathological gait analysis for spinal cord injury (SCI) via PathoFM, an encoder-centric transformer pretrained on multivariate gait windows with three complementary objectives: Local Completion (reconstruct contiguous masked spans to enforce local structure), Temporal Continuity (predict a masked mid-horizon continuation from an observed prefix to enforce smoothness and causal consistency), and Unsupervised In-Context Dynamics (support-query reconstruction conditioned on subject exemplar windows via attention). Empirically comparing objective families (grouping/contrastive, dynamics-based, and generative reconstruction), we find that dynamics-centric mixtures produce the most balanced transfer: grouping objectives favor discriminative margins but can degrade magnitude fidelity needed for continuous targets, whereas reconstruction-only objectives preserve waveform structure but may underperform on classification. Overall, combining local reconstruction with temporal continuity, and adding in-context conditioning when exemplar access is realistic, yields robust subject-generalizing representations.

### [116] [The Bridge-Garden Dilemma in LLM Distillation: Why Mixing Hard and Soft Labels Works](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26246)
*Guanghui Wang,Kaiwen Lv Kacuila,Zhiyong Yang,Zitai Wang,Jin-Wen Wu,Longtao Huang,Qianqian Xu,Qingming Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“桥-花园”分解理论，揭示了混合硬/软标签蒸馏通过缓解“暴露偏差”提升语言模型性能的内在机制，并据此开发出一种自适应混合监督方法，在大幅降低训练成本的同时显著提升了蒸馏效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现，在语言模型知识蒸馏中，单一使用硬标签或软标签均存在局限性。虽然软标签包含更丰富的信息，但混合硬软标签的效果却始终更好，且其提升原因并非简单的教师匹配度提高，而是源于对“暴露偏差”（即训练与推理分布不匹配）的抑制。本文旨在揭示这一现象背后的机理，并提出更优的蒸馏策略。

Method: 作者提出了“桥-花园”分解理论（Bridge-Garden Decomposition theory），将生成步骤分为“桥”（需要精确匹配的步骤）和“花园”（可灵活选择的步骤）。基于此理论，作者设计了一系列桥-花园混合监督方法（Bridge-Garden hybrid supervision methods），能够根据生成任务的特性自适应地平衡硬标签和软标签。

Result: 实验表明，该混合监督方法在七组主流教师-学生模型（如Qwen, Llama, Gemma, DeepSeek等）及推理与编码基准测试中，表现均优于现有的发散度基准（divergence-based）和策略上（on-policy）蒸馏方法。此外，该方法在显著降低（9.7倍）训练成本的同时，实现了高效的模型压缩。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“桥-花园”分解理论成功解释了混合硬标签与软标签知识蒸馏效果更优的根本原因，即通过自适应策略平衡精确匹配（桥）与灵活性（花园），有效缓解了语言模型训练中的暴露偏差（Exposure Bias）问题，为高效模型压缩提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers knowledge from a large teacher model to a smaller student. In language modeling, the student is trained either on tokens sampled from the teacher (hard labels) or the teacher's full next-token distribution (soft labels). Despite soft labels appear strictly richer, we find that mixing hard and soft labels consistently yields better results. Crucially, we show that this gain cannot be explained by closer teacher matching during training. Instead, it comes from reduced exposure bias, the mismatch between training and inference distributions. To explain this phenomenon, we introduce the Bridge-Garden Decomposition theory, which categorizes generation steps into two types: Bridges, where the next token must be exact, and Gardens, where it can be flexible. We show that hard-only KD excels in Bridges by avoiding risky deviations, while soft-only KD preserves diversity in Gardens. A hybrid strategy handles both cases and, as a result, reduces exposure bias across the sequence. Guided by this theory, we develop a family of Bridge-Garden hybrid supervision methods that adaptively balance hard and soft labels. Across a primary suite of seven teacher-student pairs (including Qwen, Llama, Gemma, and DeepSeek) and benchmarks in reasoning and coding, our approach outperforms divergence-based and on-policy KD baselines while reducing training cost by 9.7x, enabling efficient model compression. Code is available at https://github.com/ghwang-s/bridge_garden_hybrid_kd_release.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经缩放定律（Neural Scaling Laws）通常过于简化，往往只关注单一维度，无法满足在实际复杂场景中模型性能随多个关键因素同时变化时的预测需求，因此需要构建一种能够捕捉多维协同缩放效应的更通用模型。

Method: 作者提出了一种被称为“统一神经缩放定律（UNSL）”的函数形式，该方法突破了以往仅关注单一变量（如参数量）的限制，能够同时处理模型参数、数据集大小、训练步数、推理步数、计算量以及各种超参数等多维变量，并通过在视觉、语言、数学和强化学习等多元任务上的实验进行验证。

Conclusion: 本文提出的UNSL模型通过统一的数学框架，证明了同时考虑多个维度（参数量、数据量、训练步数、计算量等）对于准确预测深度学习模型性能至关重要，为大规模模型在复杂任务下的性能评估和扩展性分析提供了更精确的工具。

Abstract: We present a functional form (that we refer to as a Unified Neural Scaling Law (UNSL)) that accurately models and extrapolates the scaling behaviors of deep neural networks as multiple dimensions all vary simultaneously (i.e. how the evaluation metric of interest varies as one simultaneously varies the number of model parameters, training dataset size, number of training steps, number of inference steps, amount of compute, and various hyperparameters) for various architectures and for each of various tasks within a varied set of upstream and downstream tasks. This set includes large-scale vision, language, math, and reinforcement learning. When compared to other functional forms for neural scaling, this functional form yields extrapolations of scaling behavior that are considerably more accurate on this set.

### [118] [Quantized Keys Steal Attention: Bias Correction for KV-Cache Compression in Video Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26266)
*Tuna Tuncer,Felix Becker,Thomas Pfeil*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对视频扩散模型KV缓存量化导致的质量退化，本文提出了Jensen偏置纠偏方法，通过数学矫正解决了量化带来的注意力分配偏差，使得模型在INT2极低比特下仍能保持高质量视频生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分块自回归视频扩散模型在生成长视频时，KV缓存会占用大量内存，而传统的量化方法会因为精度损失严重影响视频生成质量，作者旨在解决量化带来的注意力偏置问题，从而在节省内存的同时保持高质量生成。

Method: 研究者分析了Softmax注意力机制中指数函数的凸性，指出量化噪声会导致缓存键（cached keys）的贡献被系统性高估（即Jensen偏置）。为此，作者提出了一种基于二阶泰勒展开的逐注意力分数纠偏方法，通过查询向量范数和量化步长动态计算修正项，无需额外内存和显著计算开销。

Result: 在MAGI-1、SkyReels-V2和HY-WorldPlay等模型上的实验表明，该纠偏方法能恢复因激进量化丢失的绝大部分质量。使用INT2量化即可达到接近BF16的视频质量，且性能优于INT4量化，同时进一步节省了50%的内存。

Conclusion: 该研究成功识别并量化了KV缓存量化在视频生成模型中的注意力权重偏差（Jensen偏置），通过提出的轻量级纠偏算法，实现了在极低比特（INT2）下保持视频生成质量，显著降低了长视频生成的内存开销，为大规模视频扩散模型的部署提供了高效方案。

Abstract: Chunk-wise autoregressive video diffusion models rely on a KV cache of previously generated chunks to avoid redundant computation, but this cache quickly becomes a memory bottleneck as videos grow longer. Methods that quantize the KV cache to low bitwidths reduce memory pressure but degrade video quality. We show that a key driver of this degradation is a systematic bias in attention weights: due to the convexity of the exponential in softmax attention, quantization noise inflates the contribution of cached keys, a phenomenon we call the Jensen bias. This effect causes quantized keys to steal attention mass from the unquantized current chunk. We derive a per-attention-score correction that removes this bias in expectation, computed on the fly from the quantization step sizes of the cached keys and the query norm. Using a second-order Taylor approximation, the additional computational overhead is negligible, and no additional memory is needed alongside the cache. Evaluated on MAGI-1, SkyReels-V2, and HY-WorldPlay at INT2 quantization, our correction recovers most of the quality lost to aggressive quantization, reaching near-BF16 video quality, and can outperform INT4 quantization while using 50% less memory.

### [119] [Scaling World-Model Reinforcement Learning Through Diffusion Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26282)
*Xiaoyuan Cheng,Wenxuan Yuan,Zhancun Mu,Yuanzhao Zhang,Yiming Yang,Hai Wang,Zhuo Sun,Che Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 MBDPO 框架，旨在解决世界模型中搜索与价值学习的结构性错位问题，通过扩散策略优化实现了高效、可扩展的策略学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于模型的强化学习方法在扩展性上存在局限，除了模型偏差和误差累积外，还存在一个关键瓶颈：搜索与价值学习之间的结构性错位。即策略改进依赖于非搜索策略生成的价值函数，导致训练不一致和学习次优。

Method: 提出了基于模型扩散策略优化（MBDPO）框架。该方法不再显式构建规划器，而是将策略优化重构为潜在世界模型中搜索轨迹上的扩散过程。通过从数据集中提取隐含能量函数来锚定策略，并利用评分场（score field）精细化策略，从而实现搜索与策略优化的统一。

Conclusion: MBDPO 通过扩散模型成功统一了世界模型中的搜索与价值学习，解决了策略优化中的不一致性问题。该研究证明了扩散策略能够有效捕捉轨迹分布，并在大规模数据集上展现出良好的扩展性，为提升基于模型的强化学习性能提供了新范式。

Abstract: Model-based reinforcement learning (RL) can be effectively supported at scale through the use of world models. However, in practice, scaling such approaches remains fundamentally limited. A commonly recognized challenge is model bias and error compounding, which degrade long-horizon predictions. Beyond these issues, we identify a more critical yet underexplored bottleneck: a structural misalignment between search and value learning in existing world model approaches. In particular, policy improvement often relies on value functions induced by a separate, non-search policy, resulting in training inconsistency and ultimately suboptimal learning. To address this limitation, we propose Model-Based Diffusion Policy Optimization (MBDPO) in world models, a framework that unifies search and policy optimization through diffusion policy representations, thereby unlocking the potential of world models for scalable policy learning. Instead of constructing an explicit planner over a learned world model, we reformulate policy optimization as a diffusion process over searched trajectories in latent world models. In this view, we extract an implicit energy function from the collected dataset that anchors the policy, enabling MBDPO to refine the score field for policy optimization while mitigating misalignment. We evaluate MBDPO across a wide range of settings, including multi-task offline pretraining, online learning, and offline-to-online fine-tuning. In the offline regime, we further investigate its scaling behavior by pretraining on large-scale datasets, observing consistent and monotonic performance gains with increasing model capacity.

### [120] [Two-Parameter Flows for Learning Population Dynamics of Physical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26285)
*Paul Schwerdtner,Tobias Blickhan,Benjamin Peherstorfer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种“双参数流”框架，能够在没有轨迹数据的情况下，仅利用不同时刻的无标签样本，高效学习高维概率密度的动态演化，并能有效模拟复杂的旋转或循环物理现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维空间中学习概率密度的动态演化通常依赖于轨迹数据，但在实际应用中，往往只能获取不同时刻的无标签采样数据，而无法直接获得连续的轨迹信息。因此，如何从静态的边际分布观测中推断出隐含的物理动力学，成为了一个亟待解决的挑战。

Method: 作者提出了一种“双参数流”（two-parameter flows）框架。该方法首先通过条件流匹配技术学习从基础分布到各时刻边际分布的映射（即采样时间传输），随后通过在合成的耦合轨迹上进行回归，提取出真实的物理时间速度场。这种方法避免了对每一步最优传输耦合的需求，并支持非梯度动力学的建模。

Result: 实验和理论证明表明，所提出的方法能够有效地扩展到高维数据集。该模型能够准确学习物理时间下的动态演化，并具备处理复杂非梯度动力学的能力，克服了传统方法在计算复杂度及对轨迹监督依赖上的局限性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功提出了一种名为“双参数流”的方法，在无需轨迹监督的情况下，从静态采样数据中有效地学习高维概率密度的物理演化动力学。该方法不仅在理论上保证了动力学的唯一性和正则性，还通过利用现有的条件流匹配技术，在保持高可扩展性的同时，能够捕捉复杂的旋转或循环物理现象。

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of learning the dynamics of high-dimensional probability densities over time using unlabeled samples, without assuming access to trajectory information. We introduce two-parameter flows that learn only sampling-time transports from a base distribution to each marginal and then extract a physics-time velocity by regressing on coupled synthetic trajectories. We prove that the resulting physics-time dynamics are unique and inherit regularity from the sampling-time transports. Because we can build on standard, well-developed conditional flow matching techniques for learning the base-to-marginal transports, our approach scales to high dimensions and avoids per-step optimal-transport couplings, while allowing admissible non-gradient dynamics that can naturally explain rotational or circulating physics phenomena.

### [121] [Stateful Inference for Low-Latency Multi-Agent Tool Calling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26289)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM推理框架在处理多智能体工具调用时，会将每轮对话视为独立请求并重复处理整个提示词，导致大量计算冗余（85%-95%的提示词在轮次间未变），严重拖累了推理效率。

Method: 提出了一种状态化推理架构：1. 采用持久化KV缓存（Persistent KV Cache）在对话轮次间保留中间状态；2. 利用基数前缀缓存（Radix Prefix Cache）处理交错的多智能体流量；3. 结合提示词查找（Prompt-lookup）推测解码技术以加速结构化输出。将推理复杂度从每轮的O(nt)优化为仅处理增量内容的O(Δt)。

Result: 在典型的智能体工作流上，相较于vLLM和SGLang，该架构在6轮任务中速度提升了2.1倍，在35轮任务的中位数轮次中速度提升了4.2倍，最终使端到端执行时间缩短了一半。

Conclusion: 通过引入状态化推理架构，本文证明了利用持久化KV缓存和前缀缓存技术可以显著降低多智能体工具调用中的计算冗余，从而在不依赖单纯缓存的情况下实现推理性能的大幅提升。

Abstract: Multi-agent tool calling is becoming the dominant interaction pattern for LLM-based systems, yet existing inference frameworks treat each tool call as an independent request, re-processing the entire conversation from scratch even though 85-95% of the prompt is unchanged from the previous turn.
  We present a stateful inference architecture that converts the $O(n_t)$ per-turn cost of conventional serving into an $O(Δ_t)$ delta-only cost: a persistent KV cache lives across turns and advances by ingesting only the new tokens, while a radix prefix cache extends this across interleaved multi-agent traffic and a prompt-lookup speculative decoder accelerates structured output. Against vLLM and SGLang on novel, fully-generated workloads, the reference implementation is $2.1\times$ faster per turn on a 6-turn agentic workflow and $4.2\times$ on the median turn of a 35-turn one, halving end-to-end wall time. The advantage comes from stateful reuse and speculation, not caching.

</details>


### [122] [Curriculum Learning for Safety Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26315)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然直接偏好优化（DPO）广泛用于大模型的安全对齐，但现有研究发现其表现脆弱且泛化性（OOD）较差。本文旨在探索课程学习（Curriculum Learning）是否能提升 DPO 安全对齐的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Staged-Competence”的课程学习框架：该框架首先将偏好数据按难度进行分级，随后采用基于模型能力的采样策略，并在训练过程中渐进式地更新参考模型（Reference Model），从而实现循序渐进的对齐过程。

Result: 在三个模型家族上验证，该方法将 OOD 有害回复率降低了 16%，越狱攻击成功率降低了 20%，同时在保持通用能力的同时几乎没有出现过度拒绝现象。此外，该方法在仅使用 75% 训练数据的情况下即可达到基线水平，并提升了安全与不安全响应之间的区分度。

Conclusion: Staged-Competence 证明了课程学习能够有效解决 DPO 在安全对齐中的脆性和泛化能力差的问题，为提升大语言模型的安全性提供了一种稳健、高效且具有泛化性的训练策略。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimisation (DPO) is widely used for safety alignment in large language models. However, prior work shows it is brittle and exhibits poor out-of-distribution (OOD) generalisation. In this paper, we investigate whether Curriculum Learning can improve the robustness of DPO-based safety alignment. We propose Staged-Competence, a curriculum-based framework that organises preference data by difficulty, employs competence-based sampling, and progressively updates the reference model during training. Averaged across three model families, Staged-Competence reduces OOD harmful response rates by 16% and jailbreak attack success rates by 20%, while preserving general capabilities with near-zero over-refusal. We further show that Staged-Competence (1) matches baseline safety with only 75% of the training data and (2) yields better separation between safe and unsafe responses. Staged-Competence is agnostic to the policy optimisation loss and can extend to other DPO variants and alignment domains. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/Sandeep5500/curriculum-learning-for-safety.

### [123] [Semigroup Consistency as a Diagnostic for Learned Physics Simulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26324)
*Lennon J. Shikhman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种新的评估指标“归一化半群误差”，用于检测物理模拟器在长期推演中是否违背时间演化的一致性（半群性质），实验证明该指标能有效预测模型的长期退化风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的物理模拟器评估方法多依赖一步或短时预测误差，难以发现系统在长时间推演或复杂动态演化中存在的组合性失效问题，而物理系统的演化本质上应符合半群性质。

Method: 提出“归一化半群误差（Normalized Semigroup Error）”作为一种事后、与模型无关的诊断指标。该方法通过比较“一步直接预测”与“两步组合预测”（即$s+t$步与先演化$s$步再演化$t$步）之间的差异，来量化物理模拟器对时间演化一致性的违反程度。

Result: 在热传导方程和Burgers方程的实验中，归一化半群误差与模型长时间推演的性能退化呈现正相关（Spearman相关系数达0.635），验证了该指标作为诊断工具的有效性；但引入半群正则化进行训练的效果并不理想。

Conclusion: 归一化半群误差是一种有效的评估诊断工具，能够识别学习型物理模拟器在长时间推演中的误差积累。然而，将其作为正则化手段引入训练过程的效果并不显著，说明该性质主要适用于事后评估，而非通用的训练目标。

Abstract: Learned physics simulators are often evaluated by one-step or short-horizon prediction error, but these metrics can miss failures in temporal composition and long-horizon rollout. For autonomous, state-complete systems, exact solution maps satisfy a semigroup law: direct evolution over $s+t$ should agree with evolution over $s$ followed by $t$. We propose normalized semigroup error as a post hoc, model-agnostic diagnostic comparing these direct and composed learned predictions. On one-dimensional heat and Burgers dynamics with time-conditioned ConvNet and FNO baselines, semigroup error is positively associated with rollout degradation, with trajectory-level Spearman correlation $ρ= 0.635$ and $95%$ CI $[0.621, 0.649]$. Semigroup regularization has mixed effects, supporting semigroup consistency primarily as an evaluation diagnostic rather than a universally beneficial training objective.

### [124] [Reparametrizing Shampoo and SOAP for Subspace Basis Updates and BFloat16 Storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26327)
*Alan Milligan,Zikun Xu,Simon Lacoste-Julien,Felix Dangel,Wu Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对Shampoo类优化器的重参数化方法，通过子空间QR分解和部分基向量更新策略，在实现BFP16存储以节省资源的同时，解决了低精度带来的性能损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Shampoo的优化方法（如KL-Shampoo, SOAP）严重依赖昂贵的FP32 QR分解，且在低精度（BFP16）存储下会导致模型性能下降，导致其在大规模预处理矩阵场景下计算与内存代价过高。

Method: 提出了一种针对预处理矩阵的重参数化方法。该方法通过将更新后的基向量与未更新的基向量相结合形成完整基，仅在子空间内执行QR分解，从而支持BFP16存储并减少计算复杂度。

Result: 该方法成功在BFP16存储下保持了算法的收敛性能，显著降低了计算与内存消耗。实验表明，该方法提升了SOAP和KL-SOAP在BFP16下的表现，使得KL-SOAP的性能能够持平甚至超越KL-Shampoo。

Conclusion: 本文提出的重参数化方法通过在子空间内进行QR分解并结合部分更新机制，有效解决了Shampoo类算法在BFP16存储下的性能衰减问题，并降低了计算与内存开销，使Shampoo类优化器在资源受限环境下更具实用价值。

Abstract: Shampoo-based methods, such as KL-Shampoo and SOAP, have demonstrated strong performance in training neural networks and rely on QR decomposition. Because existing QR implementations require single-precision (FP32) arithmetic and remain computationally expensive, these methods become time- and memory-intensive when their preconditioning matrices are large. Moreover, using BFloat16 (BFP16) storage to reduce memory usage can degrade the performance of Shampoo-based methods. We propose a reparametrization of the preconditioner that supports BFP16 storage and forms a complete basis by combining updated basis vectors with unchanged ones. By updating only part of the basis through QR decomposition in a subspace, our approach reduces computational overhead while mitigating the performance degradation caused by BFP16 storage. Our approach applies broadly to Shampoo-based methods that employ QR decomposition, including KL-Shampoo, SOAP, and KL-SOAP. In particular, it improves the performance of SOAP and KL-SOAP under BFP16 storage, enabling KL-SOAP to match or exceed KL-Shampoo. Overall, our approach makes Shampoo-based methods more memory- and time-efficient.

### [125] [QAM-W: Joint 2D Codebook Quantization for LLM Weights via Hadamard Rotation and Activation-Aware Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26339)
*Preetam Sharma,Kacper Dobek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决权重量化中丢失坐标相关性的问题，本文提出了 QAM-W 编解码方案。通过 Hadamard 旋转和二维配对量化，QAM-W 在 5-6 bpw 的区间内实现了媲美 W8A8 的高精度表现，并显著优于传统的极坐标编码方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的标量后训练量化方法（scalar post-training quantizers）在量化过程中忽略了权重行内坐标间的相关性结构，导致信息丢失严重。该论文旨在恢复并利用这种结构，以在极低比特率下实现更接近原始 BF16 精度的高质量权重量化。

Method: QAM-W 提出了一套包含以下步骤的压缩流程：1) 对权重行进行 L2 归一化；2) 应用分块 Hadamard 旋转以打乱并重组坐标结构；3) 将旋转后的数据两两配对，映射为二维坐标；4) 使用基于单位圆高斯分布训练的 Lloyd-Max 码本进行量化；5) 结合激活感知（activation-aware）的逐通道缩放技术，以进一步减小量化带来的精度损失。

Result: 实验表明，在涵盖 5 个大语言模型（1.1B-13B）和 8 种配置的交叉模型研究中，QAM-W 在约 5.5 bpw 下表现稳健，性能与 SmoothQuant W8A8 相当，但权重量减少了 32%。联合二维编码在相同比特率下比极坐标编码的困惑度指标高出 2-15 个百分点。在 3.5 bpw 下对量化容忍度高的架构效果良好。

Conclusion: QAM-W 是一种高效的权重量化编解码方案，特别在 5-6 bits/weight (bpw) 的区间内表现出色，能够在保持与基准 BF16 模型极高相似度（困惑度偏差在 ±0.4% 以内）的同时，相比传统方法显著降低模型存储需求。此外，联合二维编码策略优于极坐标编码，且其量化失真与 KL 散度的相关性极高。

Abstract: Scalar post-training quantizers discard pairwise coordinate structure within weight rows. We introduce QAM-W (Quadrature Amplitude Modulation for Weights), a codec that recovers this structure: each row is L2-normalized, block-Hadamard rotated, paired into 2D coordinates, and quantized against a single Lloyd-Max codebook trained on the unit circular Gaussian, with activation-aware per-channel scaling. In a cross-model study spanning five LLMs from four families (1.1B--13B parameters) and eight quantized configurations, the activation-aware variant at $\approx 5.5$ bpw stays within $\pm 0.4\%$ of BF16 WikiText-2 perplexity on every model, matching the SmoothQuant W8A8 quality envelope at $32\%$ fewer weight bits. Joint 2D coding outperforms polar (amplitude $\times$ phase) coding by 2--15~pp $Δ$PPL at equal bitrate, and paired KL against BF16 tracks $Δ$PPL\% at Spearman $ρ= 0.99$ across 37 (method, model) rows, consistent with a monotone composite bound from codec distortion to KL divergence. A 3.5~bpw variant is competitive on quantization-tolerant architectures. At strict 4~bpw, the rotated-codebook frontier method QTIP outperforms QAM-W; the contribution is the quality-preserving 5--6~bpw band.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将电路发现建模为强化学习问题，以GPT-2 Small的144个注意力头为离散动作空间；智能体通过对比奖励函数（平衡任务性能损失与通用预测能力损失）进行训练；利用PPO算法在多任务环境下进行策略优化，并在测试阶段通过“五选优”规划定位关键头。

Result: 该方法在训练任务（诱导任务和IOI任务）上达到了Oracle级别的性能，并在未见过的任务（文档字符串补全）上实现了96%的Oracle上限恢复；智能体识别出的关键头与现有文献中公认的因果非冗余头高度重合。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability has identified small sets of attention heads that implement specific behaviours in transformer language models, but recovering these circuits typically requires a bespoke analytical pipeline for each new task. We recast circuit discovery as a reinforcement-learning problem. An agent operates over the 144 attention heads of GPT-2 small as a discrete action space; each action triggers a zero-ablation and a contrastive reward that subtracts the ablation's damage to general next-token prediction from its damage to the target task. A single PPO policy, trained on two tasks (induction and IOI) in a vectorised multi-task environment, attains the per-episode oracle on both training tasks and on a held-out third task (docstring completion). Its preferred heads coincide with the canonical heads of established literature on precisely the axes those papers identify as causally non-redundant under single-head ablation; the categories they identify as redundant are correctly de-prioritised by the agent. On the held-out task, best-of-five planning recovers 96\% of the oracle ceiling with no task signal supplied at evaluation. These results indicate that reinforcement learning over causal interventions is a viable, transferable substrate for identifying the single-head bottlenecks of mechanistic circuits, complementary to existing path-patching approaches.

### [127] [When Correct Demonstrations Hurt: Rethinking the Role of Exemplars in In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26350)
*Chenghao Qiu,Chunli Peng,Yufeng Yang,Kuan-Hao Huang,Yi Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了上下文学习中的“正确性-效用差距”：正确的示例不一定有效。通过引入“任务保持扰动”方法，研究发现示例的干扰会引发“上下文证据偏移”，从而损害模型推理，表明提升ICL鲁棒性需要超越“示例正确性”的考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示上下文学习（ICL）中一个反直觉的现象：演示示例的“正确性”并不等同于其“效用”。部分正确的示例反而会降低模型性能，作者希望探索这种“正确性-效用差距”背后的原因及机制。

Method: 引入了“任务保持扰动”（task-preserving perturbations）框架，即在保持任务映射关系的前提下，仅对演示示例的输入进行修改。通过该方法，作者对比了标签更新扰动（改变语义并重算标签）与目标保持扰动（保持原标签），并提出了“上下文证据偏移”（contextual evidence shift）理论来解释性能下降的原因。

Result: 实验证明，即便演示示例完全符合任务逻辑，经过扰动后仍可能导致ICL性能显著下降。该现象在小参数模型、高难度任务及高扰动比例下尤为明显，证实了模型上下文推理容易受到示例形式化呈现方式的干扰。

Conclusion: ICL的鲁棒性不仅取决于演示示例的正确性，更在于示例如何影响模型的上下文推理过程。研究表明，仅仅保证示例正确并不能确保性能，开发者需关注示例对上下文证据分布的干扰。

Abstract: In-context learning (ICL) is often motivated by the intuition that demonstrations help because they provide correct input-output examples. However, we reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon: correctness does not guarantee exemplar utility, and some correct demonstrations can even reduce ICL accuracy. To study this correctness-utility gap, we introduce task-preserving perturbations, where only the exemplar input is changed, while the example remains a correct instance of the same task. Concretely, each perturbed exemplar is assigned the target induced by the task mapping. This framework covers both label-updating perturbations, where task-relevant semantics change and targets are recomputed, and stricter target-preserving perturbations, where the original target remains valid. We formalize the resulting failure mode as contextual evidence shift: task-preserving perturbations can change the effective mixture of evidence used by the model for contextual inference, thereby separating exemplar correctness from exemplar utility. Across sentiment classification, logical reasoning, and math word problems, we find that task-preserving perturbed demonstrations can substantially degrade ICL performance, especially for smaller models, harder tasks, and higher perturbation ratios. Our results show that robust ICL requires evaluating not only whether demonstrations are correct, but also how they influence contextual inference. Code is available at https://github.com/Chenghao-Qiu/Task-Preserving-ICL.

</details>


### [128] [Energy-Gated Attention and Wavelet Positional Encoding: Complementary Inductive Biases for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26355)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过提出能量门控注意力（EGA）和莫莱小波位置编码（MoPE），为Transformer引入了能量显著性和尺度局部性归纳偏置，显著优于传统注意力机制，并揭示了两者的超加性互补关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer注意力机制在计算时未能区分不同Token的显著性，也缺乏对不同位置在不同频率尺度下的局部适应性，导致其忽略了输入数据的固有信息结构。因此，作者旨在引入缺失的归纳偏置以改进注意力机制。

Method: 本文提出了两个核心组件：1. 能量门控注意力（EGA），通过单线性投影学习关键Token的能量估计，对值聚合进行门控，以选择关注对象；2. 莫莱小波位置编码（MoPE），利用自适应的Gaussian加窗小波替代固定的正弦位置编码，以在不同频率尺度上动态调整位置影响力。

Result: 在TinyShakespeare数据集上的实验表明，EGA提升了模型表现，MoPE作为独立组件效果有限，但两者结合实现了显著的超加性提升（+0.119的验证损失改进），且消融实验证明了学习型组件优于受约束的结构化频谱先验。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过引入能量显著性（Energy Salience）和尺度选择性局部性（Scale-selective Locality）这两种互补的归纳偏置，Transformer模型能够有效提升性能。能量门控注意力（EGA）和莫莱小波位置编码（MoPE）的结合呈现出“超加性”协同效应，证明了在模型中显式建模信息重要性和位置局部性是优于传统通用注意力的优化方向。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise token similarity but treats all tokens as equally salient and all positions as equally local, regardless of the informational structure of the input. We identify two complementary inductive biases that standard attention lacks: energy salience (which tokens concentrate informational energy, learned end-to-end without explicit frequency decomposition) and scale-selective locality (how far positional influence extends at each frequency, implemented via Morlet wavelet encoding). We address both with two simple components. Energy-Gated Attention (EGA) gates value aggregation by a learned energy estimate of key token embeddings, computed via a single linear projection; it selects what to attend to. Morlet Positional Encoding (MoPE) replaces fixed sinusoidal encodings with learned Gaussian-windowed wavelets that adapt the joint position-frequency localization to the corpus; it specifies where attention operates at each scale. On TinyShakespeare, EGA alone achieves +0.092 validation loss improvement over standard attention (+0.103 over Phase 1-3 baseline); MoPE alone is -0.032 (below baseline as a standalone encoding); but their combination achieves +0.119 -- more than the sum of parts. This superadditivity, observed across two independent training runs, is the central empirical finding: salience and locality are complementary inductive biases, each addressing a gap the other cannot fill alone. Ablations confirm that structured spectral priors (Morlet wavelet gates, scale-initialized heads, fixed sinusoidal PE) consistently underperform their unconstrained learned counterparts, while complementary learned components interact superadditively. All experiments are at small scale (<=6M parameters, character-level benchmarks, single seed); larger-scale multi-seed validation is the most important direction for future work.

</details>


### [129] [Balancing Plasticity and Stability with Fast and Slow Successor Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26357)
*Raymond Chua,Doina Precup,Blake Richards*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了强化学习在连续非平稳环境下的适应性问题，提出通过多时间尺度巩固后继特征（SFs）而非 Q 值，能有效提升智能体在渐进式变化环境中的性能，验证了稳定性在持续学习中的核心作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习智能体在应对非平稳环境（尤其是现实中常见的渐进式环境漂移）时表现不佳，且现有研究多关注突发性变化，忽视了连续非平稳性对稳定-可塑性困境的影响。

Method: 1. 构建了包含自然、连续非平稳性的 3D Miniworld 和 MuJoCo 基准环境；2. 对比了强调稳定性（如突触巩固）与强调可塑性（如参数重置）的方法；3. 提出了基于后继特征（Successor Features, SFs）的突触巩固方法，并引入多时间尺度稳定机制。

Result: 实验表明，在连续变化的设置中，侧重稳定性的突触巩固方法优于侧重可塑性的方法；将巩固目标从 Q 值转向后继特征（SFs），并结合多时间尺度稳定，显著提升了智能体在非平稳环境下的适应能力和性能。

Conclusion: 在面对环境逐渐演变的连续非平稳性任务时，稳定性比可塑性更为关键。通过多时间尺度对后继特征（SFs）进行神经启发的突触巩固，是实现持续学习并解决稳定-可塑性困境的有效策略。

Abstract: A hallmark of intelligence is the ability to adapt in non-stationary environments, yet deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents often struggle in such settings. Prior studies introduce non-stationarity through abrupt shifts in features or dynamics, whereas real-world environments often evolve gradually through continual drift. This distinction has important implications for the "stability-plasticity dilemma" in RL, as abrupt task changes may demand more plasticity than naturalistic settings. To address this, we modify existing 3D Miniworld and MuJoCo environments to incorporate naturalistic, continual non-stationarity, and use them to examine how stability and adaptation affect performance under continuous environmental change. We find that methods favoring stability, such as synaptic consolidation, outperform approaches focused on plasticity, such as parameters resetting. Motivated by this result, and prior evidence that Successor Features (SFs) reduce interference, we investigate whether SFs are better consolidation targets than Q-values. Across both environments, applying neuro-inspired synaptic consolidation to SFs yields superior performance on continually changing settings. Moreover, consolidation is most effective when SFs are stabilized across multiple timescales, which capture complementary aspects of gradual environmental change. Together, these results suggest that stability is more critical in continual learning when changes are gradual, and that multi-timescale consolidation of predictive representations is an effective approach.

</details>


### [130] [Online Learning on Hidden-Convex Losses via Algorithmic Equivalence: Optimal Regret, Geometric Barrier, and Bandit Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26373)
*Anas Barakat,Andreas Kontogiannis,Vasilis Pollatos,Ioannis Panageas,Antonios Varvitsiotis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究解决了隐凸优化中的两个核心问题：一是通过改进算法分析，使在线梯度下降（OGD）在隐凸损失下达到了在线凸优化的最优 $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret 界；二是通过引入“黑塞矩阵兼容性”条件，精确刻画了保证该性能所需的几何结构，并将其扩展到了老虎机反馈设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的研究（Ghai, Lu and Hazan, 2022）表明在隐凸损失下使用 OGD 只能达到 $\mathcal{O}(T^{2/3})$ 的 regret，尚未达到在线凸优化的最优 $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ 界。此外，该领域缺乏对于实现算法等价性所需几何条件的清晰定义，需要进一步探索参数化条件的必要性与充分性。

Method: 1. 采用离散时间的算法等价性论证，将隐凸损失的 OGD 行为映射到底层凸损失的在线镜像下降（OMD）；2. 使用黑塞矩阵兼容性条件替代了原有的对角雅可比矩阵假设，扩展了可行参数化的范围；3. 构建对抗性损失序列，通过下界分析证明了黑塞兼容性条件的必要性；4. 利用球形平滑技术将分析扩展至单点老虎机反馈设置。

Result: 1. 在与之前相同的假设下，证明了 OGD 在隐凸损失下可达到 $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ 的最优 regret。2. 确立了“黑塞矩阵兼容性”作为实现该算法等价性的必要且充分条件。3. 证明了若该条件不满足，OGD 可能遭受线性（$\Omega(T)$）的 regret。4. 在单点老虎机反馈下，实现了 $\mathcal{O}(T^{3/4})$ 的期望 regret。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了在隐凸损失函数设置下，通过在线梯度下降（OGD）可以达到与在线凸优化相同的最优 regret 界（$\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$）。此外，该研究通过提出必要且充分的“黑塞矩阵兼容性”（Hessian compatibility）条件，界定了算法等价性的几何边界，并为多臂老虎机反馈提供了相应的 regret 上界。

Abstract: We study adversarial online learning with hidden-convex losses, i.e., nonconvex losses that become convex after a nonlinear reparameterization. Ghai, Lu and Hazan (2022) proved that, under geometric and smoothness assumptions, online gradient descent (OGD) on such nonconvex losses approximately simulates online mirror descent (OMD) on the underlying convex losses with a suitable regularizer, yielding $\mathcal{O}(T^{2/3})$ regret. They left open whether the optimal $Θ(\sqrt{T})$ regret from online convex optimization can be recovered in this hidden-convex setting. We answer this question affirmatively. More specifically, via a sharper discrete-time algorithmic equivalence argument, we prove that OGD achieves $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{T})$ regret under the same assumptions, matching the optimal worst-case rate for adversarial online convex optimization. We also address another open question of Ghai, Lu and Hazan (2022) by clarifying the geometry required for this algorithmic equivalence. We replace the diagonal-Jacobian sufficient condition with a necessary-and-sufficient Hessian compatibility condition, thereby expanding the class of admissible reparameterizations. We complement our tight regret bound with a lower bound showing that the Hessian compatibility assumption is essential for OGD; when it fails, we construct a smooth reparameterization and an adversarial sequence of hidden-convex losses for which OGD suffers $Ω(T)$ regret. Finally, we extend our analysis to one-point bandit feedback and prove a $\mathcal{O}(T^{3/4})$ expected regret bound for bandit OGD with spherical smoothing, matching its classical rate on convex losses.

</details>


### [131] [When Does Deep RL Beat Calibrated Baselines? A Benchmark Study on Adaptive Resource Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26418)
*Guilin Zhang,Chuanyi Sun,Kai Zhao,Shahryar Sarkani,John Fossaceca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过构建基准测试 RLScale-Bench，证明了经过校准的规则基准在资源伸缩任务中表现往往优于主流深度强化学习（DRL）算法，并指出强化学习在实际部署中的主要挑战在于奖励工程与基准校准而非算法选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者观察到在学术界和工业界，深度强化学习（DRL）常被视为解决动态资源分配问题的银弹，但缺乏与经过充分调优的规则基准进行公平比较的证据。因此，研究旨在量化 DRL 在自动伸缩中的实际效能，探究其相比传统方法是否具备显著优势及局限性。

Method: 作者构建了名为 RLScale-Bench 的基准测试框架，在 Kubernetes 水平 Pod 自动伸缩（HPA）环境下，对比了 PPO、DQN、A2C、SAC、TD3 和 DDPG 六种深度强化学习算法与经过校准的规则基准。测试涵盖了六种不同的工作负载模式，通过 240 次实验评估了在成本和性能约束下的资源分配能力及分布偏移（distribution-shift）的泛化性能。

Result: 实验发现：（1）经过校准的规则基准在所有测试负载下的总成本均优于 DRL 算法，仅在突发流量场景下略逊色；（2）离散动作空间的算法在约束违规率上优于连续动作空间算法，主要源于动作空间匹配度差异；（3）没有一种 DRL 算法在所有负载下均表现领先，算法排序随负载变化剧烈，泛化能力较差。

Conclusion: 在资源自动伸缩领域，当前强化学习算法并未展现出普遍优于成熟规则基准的优势。RL算法面临的真正瓶颈不在于算法本身的选择，而在于基准校准、奖励函数设计以及缺乏严谨的评估协议。未来的研究应侧重于提升模型的通用性，而非盲目追求算法的复杂化。

Abstract: A properly calibrated rule-based autoscaler can beat every one of six mainstream deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms on cost across every workload we test - so when, if ever, does DRL actually help? We study this in RLScale-Bench, a reproducible benchmark and evaluation protocol for DRL on adaptive resource control, where an agent allocates compute to a dynamic workload under cost and service-level constraints. We evaluate PPO, DQN, A2C, SAC, TD3, and DDPG under matched architectures, training budgets, and reward functions against a calibrated rule-based baseline across six workload patterns and five seeds (240 runs), instantiate the benchmark on Kubernetes Horizontal Pod Autoscaling, and probe distribution-shift generalization. Three findings challenge common assumptions: (i) the calibrated controller achieves the lowest cost on all six workloads, though it trails the best RL agents on bursty and flash traffic; (ii) discrete-action algorithms outperform continuous-action ones by one to two orders of magnitude in constraint violations due to action-space mismatch; and (iii) no single algorithm dominates across workloads, with rankings shifting by up to four positions. The bottleneck in RL-based resource control is not algorithm selection but baseline calibration, reward engineering, and realistic evaluation protocols.

*Peiyu Duan,Jiyao Wang,Nicha C. Dvornek,Junlin Yang,Ziqi Gao,Lawrence H. Staib,James S. Duncan*

Method: 该研究提出了 FM-fMRI，这是一种事件条件化的流匹配模型。它通过学习连续时间条件向量场，将受试者的静息态 fMRI 和任务事件信息映射为任务 ROI 时间序列。该方法利用常微分方程（ODE）进行快速采样，并具备对异构任务时间表的灵活条件化能力，优于传统的扩散模型、GAN 和 VAE。

Result: 在 Human Connectome Project 和 BioPoint 自闭症队列上的测试表明，FM-fMRI 在频谱一致性、连接组一致性和分布对齐度方面均优于现有基准模型。此外，通过合成任务态 fMRI 数据增强样本，显著提高了自闭症分类的准确率，验证了其在数据匮乏临床场景下的实际应用价值。

Conclusion: FM-fMRI 证明了基于流匹配（Flow-matching）的方法在从静息态 fMRI 生成任务态信号方面的卓越性能。该模型不仅能生成高质量、高保真的任务 fMRI 数据，还通过数据增强有效提升了临床诊断任务（如自闭症分类）的性能，为解决医学影像数据稀缺问题提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Task-based fMRI provides a direct readout of task-evoked neural dynamics, but it is expensive and difficult to acquire at scale, motivating rest-to-task synthesis from widely available resting-state fMRI (rsfMRI). We propose FM-fMRI, an event-conditioned flow-matching model that learns a continuous-time conditional vector field to generate task ROI time series from a subject's rsfMRI and the task event information. The formulation enables fast ODE-based sampling and flexible conditioning over heterogeneous event schedules. Rather than optimizing for pointwise reconstruction, we evaluated generated signals using complementary criteria that probe temporal and spectral structure, subject and group-level connectome consistency, and distributional alignment. On the public Human Connectome Project and internal BioPoint autism cohort, FM-fMRI achieves the strongest spectral and connectivity agreement and improved distribution-level matching over conditional diffusion, generative adversarial networks (GANs), and variational autoencoders (VAEs) baselines. Furthermore, we augment the BioPoint cohort by synthesizing task-fMRI ROI time series with our method, improving downstream autism classification and demonstrating practical utility in data-limited clinical settings. The code will be available on GitHub.

*Aditya Kommineni,Emily Zhou,Kleanthis Avramidis,Simon Bock Segaard,Jeppe Roden Münster,Andreas Peter Juhl Hansen,Takfarinas Medani,Tiantian Feng,Richard Leahy,Shrikanth Narayanan*

TL;DR: 本文指出重构类EEG基础模型因忽视高频振荡信号而存在泛化瓶颈，并建议通过引入辅助任务来改进对关键振荡特征的捕捉。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用受控的合成EEG数据进行机制分析，通过定量评估模型在捕捉非周期性与振荡性成分上的差异，并结合线性探针（linear probe）在实际脑机接口（BCI）数据集上的表现，分析了模型对受试者身份的过拟合现象及其对低频信号的偏好。

Result: 实验表明，EEG基础模型嵌入层明显偏向于捕捉信号中的非周期性成分，而严重低估了高频振荡成分。此外，这些模型在真实数据中表现出更强的受试者身份编码倾向，进一步加剧了对低频非周期信息的依赖，导致在具体任务处理上泛化能力不足。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了基于重构任务的脑电图（EEG）基础模型存在显著的局限性，即模型偏向于学习非周期性成分而忽略了高频振荡成分。这一发现强调了在EEG表征学习中引入针对性辅助损失函数的重要性，为构建更通用、高效的EEG基础模型指明了改进方向。

Abstract: EEG foundation models, pre-trained on large-scale unlabelled EEG data, have emerged as a promising direction towards learning generalizable EEG representations. Despite showing positive results in data-rich regimes, they often fail to outperform significantly smaller supervised models in low-resource settings compared to fully supervised models. We provide a mechanistic account of this shortcoming, attributing it to a fundamental mismatch between reconstruction-based pretext tasks and the idiosyncratic spectral structure of EEG signals, which decompose into distinct high-power aperiodic and low-power oscillatory components. Using controlled, synthetically-generated EEG inputs, we demonstrate that EEG foundation model embeddings are biased to capture the aperiodic components of the EEG signal while under-representing oscillatory components, particularly at higher frequencies. Additionally, linear probe evaluations on real-world BCI datasets further reveal that embeddings encode subject identity more strongly than task-relevant information, thereby reinforcing the low-frequency and aperiodic component bias in foundation model embeddings trained primarily on reconstruction based objectives. Together, these findings elucidate a failure mode in reconstruction based EEG foundation models and motivate future work to incorporate auxiliary losses explicitly targeting high-frequency oscillatory structure as a path toward more capable and generalizable EEG representations.

### [134] [MuCon: Clipped Muon Updates for LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26459)
*Albert Yi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了MuCon优化器，通过对Muon算法中的奇异值进行裁剪而非强制归一化来提升训练灵活性，并深入分析了如何通过矩阵函数高效近似计算该过程及其面临的数值不稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器通过将矩阵映射到正交方向（将所有非零奇异值强制置为1）来优化权重，这在某些情况下可能过于激进。本文旨在研究通过“裁剪”而非“归一化”奇异值（即MuCon）能否在保持优化的同时，通过近似计算方法减少昂贵的密集奇异值分解（SVD）计算成本。

Method: 作者引入了MuCon算法，通过奇异值裁剪算子（MClip）代替Muon优化器中的极分解算子，旨在将奇异值限制在阈值τ以内。文中还分析了两种用于近似该裁剪步骤的数学公式（极性/绝对值公式与标量根公式，后者导向有理牛顿滤波器），并分析了其数值条件。

Result: 论文推导了MuCon裁剪算子的精确恒等式，揭示了矩阵函数法在处理奇异值接近阈值时的病态问题，明确了实现高效且数值稳定的MuCon近似计算所需的算法约束条件。

Conclusion: 本文指出了在MuCon优化器中进行矩阵奇异值裁剪（MClip）时存在的数值不稳定性，特别是当奇异值接近阈值时会导致计算病态。因此，矩阵函数方法需要与稳定的极分解或平方根原语结合，或在裁剪边界附近进行显式正则化才能有效应用。

Abstract: Muon-style optimizers take a matrix-valued momentum or preconditioned update $B = U \operatorname{diag}(σ_1,\ldots,σ_r) V^\top$ and replace it with its canonical partial polar factor $\operatorname{Pol}(B) = U V^\top$. This maps every nonzero singular value to one. MuCon is the clipped-Muon variant studied here: it applies singular-value clipping to the same Muon matrix, $D^{\mathrm{MuCon}}\_τ(B) = \operatorname{MClip}\_τ(B) = U \operatorname{diag}\bigl(\min\{σ\_i,τ\}\bigr) V^\top, \qquad τ> 0$. Thus, $\operatorname{MClip}\_τ$ denotes the mathematical clipping operator, while MuCon denotes the optimizer primitive that substitutes this clipped direction for Muon's polar direction. The Muon/MuCon scaling parameterization used in this work is called $\text{SpectralP}$: it is the hidden-matrix scaling recipe under which polar Muon or clipped MuCon directions are applied. The map $\operatorname{MClip}\_τ$ is the Frobenius projection onto the spectral-norm ball $\{X : \|X\|_2 \le τ\}$: it leaves singular values at or below $τ$ unchanged and modifies only the violating singular directions. This paper asks when the MuCon clipping step can be approximated without a full dense SVD. We record two exact identities, a polar/absolute-value formula and a scalar-root formulation leading to a rational Newton filter for the clipped positive-semidefinite factor, and identify the numerical obstruction common to both: singular values near the threshold make sign decisions and rational solves ill-conditioned. Matrix-function methods are therefore useful only when paired with stable polar/square-root primitives or explicit regularization near the clipping boundary.

</details>

Raw test measurements are first compressed by an autoencoder, then reshaped into a structured token sequence enriched with sinusoidal and per-device wafer-position embeddings. Anomaly scores are derived from the noise-prediction error over mid-range diffusion timesteps, enabling fast wafer-scale screening without any labeled defects or manual feature engineering. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance on industrial 16nm IC test data under extreme class imbalance, offering interpretable failure localization through latent-space reconstruction residuals.

### [136] [Extra-Merge: Tracing the Rank-1 Subspace of Model Merging in Language Model Pre-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26484)
*Wenjie Zhou,Bohan Wang,Hongtao Zhang,Chenxi Jia,Wei Chen,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现预训练后期权重存在“Rank-1子空间”，利用这一几何特性提出的Extra-Merge策略，可在无需训练的情况下通过线性外推显著提升大模型性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管模型合并（Model Merging）在大模型领域应用广泛，但其提升性能的内在机制尚不明确，缺乏系统的理论解释和有效的指导策略。

Method: 1. 轨迹分析：通过分析预训练后期的权重轨迹，发现合并检查点会坍缩至一维线性流形；2. 理论建模：提出“河谷”景观分析，将模型平均视为一种滤除高曲率噪声的几何低通滤波器；3. Extra-Merge策略：提出一种基于该子空间的训练无关外推算法，在不进行梯度更新的情况下直接寻找更优的权重解。

Result: 在GPT-2和LLaMA系列（124M至2B参数）模型上的实验表明，Extra-Merge优于现有的标准合并基线，在Pythia-12B模型下游任务中实现了零样本精度的提升，并对Muon优化器具有良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了模型合并中“Rank-1子空间”现象，并证明通过利用这一几何特性，无需额外训练即可有效优化模型性能，为理解大模型权重演化规律提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Model merging has emerged as a lightweight paradigm for enhancing Large Language Models (LLMs), yet its underlying mechanisms remain poorly understood. In this work, we analyze late-stage pre-training trajectories and uncover a \textbf{Rank-1 Subspace} phenomenon: while raw optimization steps oscillate violently, consecutive \emph{merged} checkpoints collapse onto a stable, approximately one-dimensional linear manifold. We theoretically ground this observation in a \emph{river-valley} landscape analysis: averaging acts as a geometric low-pass filter that dampens high-curvature noise to reveal the optimal descent direction. Capitalizing on this insight, we propose \textbf{Extra-Merge}, a training-free strategy that extrapolates along this subspace to minimize loss without additional gradient updates. Extensive experiments across GPT-2 and LLaMA families (124M to 2B) demonstrate that Extra-Merge consistently outperforms standard merging baselines. Notably, it yields consistent zero-shot accuracy gains on Pythia-12B downstream tasks and generalizes effectively to the Muon optimizer \citep{jordan2024muon}.

</details>


### [137] [The Stability of Singular Distribution: A Spectral Perspective on the Two-Phase Dynamics of Language Model Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26489)
*Hongtao Zhang,Wenjie Zhou,Chenxi Jia,Wei Chen,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大语言模型预训练中“奇异值分布稳定性”（SoSD）现象，指出其是导致模型训练后期收敛变慢的关键机制，并通过光谱视角解释了当前高效预训练策略的工作原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型预训练通常呈现出“先快后慢”的损失下降轨迹，但这种现象背后的深层动力学机制尚不明确。研究者旨在通过分析参数矩阵的奇异值谱，探究是什么物理机制导致了训练后期的慢速改进，从而为优化预训练过程提供理论指导。

Method: 本文采用了理论分析与实证研究相结合的方法。首先，通过对 GPT-2 和 LLaMA 等多种主流架构进行光谱分析，验证了 SoSD 现象的普遍性；其次，通过简化 Transformer 模型进行数学推导，证明了权重范数增长与 SoSD 阈值之间的必然联系；最后，利用该光谱视角分析了 WSD 和 Muon 等优化策略对预训练动力学的影响。

Result: 研究发现，参数矩阵的迹归一化奇异值谱在训练早期即趋于稳定，即“奇异值分布稳定性”（SoSD）；SoSD 与训练进入慢速下降阶段高度同步，且该现象在不同模型架构、学习率调度和优化器配置中广泛存在；理论推导证明，权重范数的持续增长不可避免地导致 SoSD 阈值的出现，此时损失下降速率受限于奇异值分布的变化。

Conclusion: 本文通过光谱分析揭示了大语言模型预训练中“奇异值分布稳定性”（SoSD）这一核心现象。研究表明，SoSD 的出现标志着模型训练进入了慢速收敛阶段。理解并调控 SoSD 现象，为优化大模型预训练策略、提升训练效率提供了明确的理论支撑和光谱视角。

Abstract: Large language model pre-training typically exhibits a two-phase trajectory: a fast initial loss drop followed by a prolonged slow improvement. We identify an underlying spectral phenomenon, Stability of Singular Distribution (SoSD), where the trace-normalized singular value spectrum stabilizes early, even as parameter matrices continue to evolve. We demonstrate that synchronization between SoSD and the slow-descent regime is widely observed across diverse architectures (GPT-2, LLaMA) and settings, including various schedules (Step-wise, WSD, Cosine Decay), weight decays, and optimizers (AdamW, Muon). By analyzing a simplified Transformer, we prove that growing weight norms inevitably precipitate an early SoSD threshold, after which the rate of loss decrease becomes theoretically bounded by the variation in the singular distribution. We further interpret strategies like WSD and Muon through their ability to modulate the SoSD scale, offering a spectral lens for understanding efficient pre-training dynamics.

### [138] [Beyond Pairwise Preferences: Listwise Reward-Aware Alignment for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26491)
*Austin Wang,Jiaqi Han,Stefano Ermon,Yisong Yue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Diffusion LAIR 提出了一种新的列表式偏好优化框架，通过将多候选样本的奖励得分转化为中心化优势权重，实现比传统成对比较更高效、更丰富的对齐效果，显著提升了扩散模型的生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型偏好优化方法主要依赖于二元成对比较，这限制了模型从多样本数据中学习的能力，且忽略了连续奖励得分所包含的丰富信息。研究旨在克服这些局限，充分利用多候选样本和连续奖励得分来优化模型性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Diffusion LAIR 的奖励感知列表式偏好优化方法。该方法将同一提示词下的多个候选图像的奖励得分转化为中心化优势权重，并基于去噪损失的提升定义隐式奖励，通过带二次惩罚项的加权回归目标函数进行优化，实现对模型偏好的整体训练，而非局限于成对比较。

Result: 在 SD1.5 和 SDXL 模型上的实验结果表明，Diffusion LAIR 在文本到图像生成、组合式生成以及图像编辑等任务中，性能均优于现有的主流偏好优化基线方法。

Abstract: Preference optimization has emerged as an efficient alternative to online reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) for aligning text-to-image diffusion models. However, existing methods largely reduce supervision to binary pairwise comparisons. This pairwise reduction is limiting when training data naturally contains multiple candidate images for the same prompt, and when continuous reward scores can provide richer information than a single winner-loser label. To address these limitations, we propose Diffusion LAIR, a reward-aware listwise preference optimization method for diffusion models. For each prompt, LAIR converts reward scores across a group of candidate images into centered advantage weights, then optimizes an advantage-weighted regression objective on the implicit reward, defined as the denoising-loss improvement of the current model over a fixed reference model, with a quadratic penalty that regularizes the magnitude of the implicit reward. The resulting objective uses all candidates simultaneously rather than selecting pairs, and remains conservative by explicitly controlling the magnitude of the implicit reward. The LAIR objective admits a bounded closed-form optimum in implicit-reward space, clarifying how the regularization strength controls the magnitude of the preference update. Experiments show that Diffusion LAIR outperforms strong preference optimization baselines on SD1.5 and SDXL across text-to-image generation, compositional generation, and image editing benchmarks.

### [139] [Dense2MoE: Pushing the Pareto Frontier of On-Device LLMs via Unified Pruning and Upcycling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26496)
*Fengfa Li,Hongjin Ji,Yifeng Ding,Lei Ren,Chen Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Dense2MoE 是一种将大型稠密 LLM 转化为端侧高效 MoE 模型的新框架，它通过剪枝注意力模块并将其 MLP 转化为 MoE 专家，成功在保持准确率的同时突破了端侧推理的内存瓶颈与延迟限制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的端侧模型部署面临挑战：从头训练 MoE 模型成本过高；现有的稠密模型转 MoE 方法常带来参数冗余，降低了推理效率；而传统的剪枝方法往往以牺牲模型准确率为代价。因此需要一种既能保持准确率又能提高推理效率的转换方法。

Method: 提出了“层融合上循环”（LF-UC）框架，并结合硬件 Roofline 理论：1. 裁剪掉带宽敏感的冗余注意力模块以优化内存瓶颈；2. 将原有的 MLP 模块重构为 MoE 的专家（Experts）；3. 采用选择性令牌路由（Selective Token Routing）技术，在保持核心能力的同时严格控制激活参数量。

Result: 实验表明，Dense2MoE 在模型推理延迟与准确率的权衡（Pareto frontier）上表现优异，显著优于稠密基准模型、现有的压缩技术以及标准的上循环方法，在保证较少持续预训练开销的前提下实现了高效的端侧部署。

Conclusion: Dense2MoE 提出了一种高效的转换框架，通过层融合与上循环（LF-UC）策略，成功将大型稠密语言模型（LLM）转换为轻量级、高性能的端侧 MoE 模型，为解决模型压缩中的准确率与推理效率权衡问题提供了新的最优方案（Pareto frontier）。

Abstract: The Mixture of Experts MoE architecture is highly promising for resource constrained on device deployments yet training these models from scratch incurs prohibitive costs Current methods attempt to alleviate this by upcycling dense models into MoEs however they often introduce parameter redundancy that degrades inference efficiency Alternatively standard layer pruning mitigates redundancy but inevitably compromises model accuracy To resolve this dilemma we propose Dense2MoE a novel framework that unifies pruning and upcycling through Layer Fusion UpCycling LF UC Guided by hardware Roofline theory Dense2MoE systematically overcomes the inference memory wall by pruning bandwidth heavy attention modules from redundant layers while repurposing their Multi Layer Perceptrons MLPs into MoE experts This structural innovation preserves the models core capabilities and strictly limits active parameters via selective token routing With a modest continual pre training budget Dense2MoE efficiently converts publicly available dense LLMs into on device ready MoE models Extensive experiments demonstrate that Dense2MoE significantly advances the Pareto frontier for on device inference latency versus model accuracy outperforming dense baselines state of the art compression and standard upcycling methods

### [140] [Open-Weight LLM Fine-Tuning Defenses are Susceptible to Simple Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26526)
*Kevin Kuo,Chhavi Yadav,Virginia Smith*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了开源LLM的安全防御存在重大漏洞，证明即便不进行恶意微调，简单的消融和预填充攻击也能轻易绕过现有的防御措施，并提出了ART策略以增强模型防御能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的开源大语言模型安全防御机制主要假设有害行为是通过微调习得的，从而忽略了模型预训练阶段已蕴含的有害知识。研究旨在探讨在不进行微调的情况下，通过简单的越狱手段是否仍能绕过这些安全防御措施。

Method: 研究团队评估了两种低成本、非梯度的攻击方法：消融攻击（abliteration）和预填充攻击（prefilling）。在三个基准测试（BeaverTails, HarmBench, AdvBench）上对受保护的开源模型进行测试，并提出了一种名为“消融抗性微调（ART）”的新型防御策略，通过将消融目标纳入训练过程以增强模型鲁棒性。

Result: 实验结果显示，通过消融和预填充攻击，受保护模型的攻击成功率从不足10%显著提升至16%-96%之间。此外，ART防御策略能够将上述攻击的成功率降低10%-20%，证明了其作为现有防御体系补充的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文研究揭示了开源大语言模型的防御机制存在严重的盲区。研究表明，现有的针对微调的防御手段不足以防止直接的越狱攻击。因此，评估防御有效性时必须包含更广泛的攻击策略，并建议采用如ART等更稳健的防御技术。

Abstract: Recent defenses for safeguarding open-weight large language models (LLMs) are intended to prevent adversarial usage. Underlying these defenses is an assumption that new harmful behavior is learned through fine-tuning rather than elicited by jailbreaking the model. Yet, pretrained LLMs already encode substantial harmful knowledge across many domains, which raises an important question: can an adversary jailbreak safeguarded models, to achieve harmful usage without fine-tuning at all? In this paper, we show that open-weight safeguards are susceptible to simpler strategies that, despite being well known, have not been systematically evaluated against these safeguards. Specifically, we evaluate two low-cost attacks--abliteration and prefilling--that do not rely on gradient-based optimization. Across three harmfulness evaluation benchmarks (BeaverTails, HarmBench, and AdvBench), these attacks increase attack success rates against safeguarded open-weight models from below 10\% to a range of 16%-96%. To mitigate this vulnerability, we introduce abliteration-resistant tuning (ART), which incorporates an abliteration-based objective into training. ART can be layered onto existing defenses and reduces the success rates of abliteration, prefilling, and their combination by 10%-20%. These findings indicate that the attack surface for open-weight models is broader than previously characterized, and that evaluations of safeguarding defenses should incorporate a more diverse set of attack strategies beyond adversarial fine-tuning.

Method: 提出了一种名为递归流匹配（Recursive Flow Matching, RecFM）的生成式框架。该方法通过引入自一致性约束，在不同离散化尺度下对轨迹进行对齐，从而显著降低离散化误差，并支持极少步数（1-4步）的高保真动力学预测。

Abstract: Generative models have emerged as a powerful paradigm for solving physics systems and modeling complex spatiotemporal dynamics. In this work, we introduce Recursive Flow Matching (RecFM), a generative framework for forecasting complex spatiotemporal dynamics. RecFM enforces self-consistency to align trajectories across discretization scales, reducing discretization errors and improving performance across metrics for physics-based tasks. To our knowledge, this is the first method to achieve high-fidelity one- and few-step (2-4 step) dynamic generation for scientific systems with performance comparable to state-of-the-art multi-step solvers. Across challenging scientific benchmarks, RecFM achieves up to a 20$\times$ speedup over leading diffusion-based emulators while improving predictive accuracy. Abstract: Contextual dueling bandits form a cornerstone of preference-based decision-making, with critical applications in
  recommender systems and large language model alignment. However, standard algorithms rely on the idealized assumption
  of immediate feedback, a condition frequently violated in real-world scenarios such as prompt optimization. This
  setting introduces a unique theoretical challenge: unlike linear bandits, dueling bandit estimators lack closed-form
  solutions, rendering naive adaptations of standard weighting techniques biased. To address this, we formalize the
  problem of Contextual Dueling Bandits with Stochastic Delayed Feedback and propose two novel algorithms: Linear

  experiments on both simulated and real-world datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of our propose.

Method: 提出了一种两阶段适配器（Two-stage adapter）方法：第一阶段构建符合经济理论约束的标准选择模型（如Logit模型）；第二阶段在保持经济参数不变的前提下，训练一个校正项，将基础模型的预测作为辅助输入，从而在保证经济逻辑一致性的同时融合基础模型的预测增益。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models achieve strong accuracy on choice prediction tasks, but their predictions often violate the economic logic those tasks require: raising a price sometimes increases predicted demand, and implied willingness-to-pay estimates are frequently negative or implausible. We propose a two-stage adapter that embeds foundation model predictions within a utility-maximization framework. In the first stage, we estimate a standard choice model whose parameters are constrained to obey economic theory. In the second stage, we freeze those parameters and train a correction term that incorporates the foundation model's predictions as additional information. The result is a model that inherits the foundation model's accuracy gains while guaranteeing monotonic price-demand relationships under policy perturbation and producing analytically computable trade-off measures. On two transportation datasets, the adapter recovers up to 13 percentage points of accuracy over a standard logit model while maintaining perfect economic consistency, something neither the raw foundation models nor conventional distillation achieve.

Motivation: 现有不确定性量化方法（如CQR或CMC）往往局限于特定的模型或分数类型，缺乏灵活性。为了解决在不同不确定性环境下难以统一高效构建预测区间的问题，研究者旨在构建一个模块化、分布感知的通用框架。

Method: 提出了“分布感知保形预测（DCP）”框架。该方法利用数值求逆技术构建区间边界，允许任意组合概率预测模型（如MC Dropout、深度集成、分位数回归）与分数不可知的保形校准方法，并通过改进的Winkler分数来评估和平衡区间的覆盖有效性与预测效率。

Result: 通过在合成数据和真实世界时间序列数据上的基准测试，证明了DCP能够针对不同的不确定性场景自适应地校准预测区间，其性能优于或扩展了现有的保形预测方法，且引入的修正Winkler分数能更好地衡量覆盖率与区间宽度的平衡。

Conclusion: DCP通过模块化设计提供了一个通用的不确定性量化框架，能够灵活集成多种概率预测模型与保形分数，有效提升了动态环境下预测区间的有效性与效率，为高风险应用提供了稳健的量化基础。

Abstract: We present Distribution-aware Conformal Prediction (DCP), a unified framework integrating probabilistic predictors like Monte Carlo dropout, deep ensembles, and quantile regression with score-agnostic conformal calibration to produce valid and efficient prediction intervals. Leveraging a numerical inversion approach to construct interval bounds, DCP accommodates arbitrary combinations of distribution generating predictors and nonconformity scores. Benchmark analysis on synthetic and real-world time series data demonstrate DCP's ability to adaptively calibrate prediction intervals under varying uncertainty regimes. Crucially, DCP's modular design facilitates plug-and-play experimentation with different predictor-score pairings, quantitatively supported by a newly introduced modified Winkler score that balances validity and efficiency by explicitly penalizing undercoverage. While DCP generalizes and extends existing approaches like Conformalized Quantile Regression and Conformalized Monte Carlo, its modular design allows further extensions, setting a foundation for advancing uncertainty quantification in dynamic environments and high-risk applications.

Existing PFL methods often face a fundamental tradeoff in which stronger global sharing can undermine local specialization, whereas stronger local adaptation can lead to overfitting under limited data, label imbalance, and missing class scenarios. In this work, we propose PGFedSplit, a personalized federated learning framework that improves both personalization and global generalization under severe client heterogeneity. PGFedSplit adopts a split architecture and performs adaptive aggregation scheduling tailored to the roles of different model components, enabling stable knowledge sharing while maintaining client specific adaptation. ### [146] [Focal Reward: Balanced Reinforcement Learning under Rubric-Based Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26579)
*Yu Huang,Zihua Zhao,Zhaoxin Huan,Wanli Gu,Feng Hong,Xinmu Ge,Lin Yuan,Weichang Wu,Qiang Hu,Xiaolu Zhang,Jun Zhou,Jiangchao Yao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在多维度奖励引导的强化学习中，常出现奖励极化现象，即模型在部分维度获得高分的同时，在其他维度表现严重不足，损害了整体用户体验。现有的静态聚合方法难以解决这种维度间的不平衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为“焦点奖励”（Focal Reward）的训练目标，通过逆奖励投影机制评估各维度奖励的饱和度，并结合自动重加权系数，实时动态地调整各维度在强化学习中的权重，引导模型优先优化尚未饱和的维度。

Result: 通过在三种模型规模和六个基准测试上的实验，证明了 Focal Reward 在所有 18 组对比实验中均优于现有的最强静态聚合基线，表现出更优的综合质量。

Conclusion: Focal Reward 有效解决了大模型强化学习中多维度奖励不平衡导致的性能偏置问题，提供了一种动态、自适应的优化方案，能够显著提升模型在多个评估维度上的综合表现，具有良好的通用性和扩展性。

Abstract: The open-ended generation in LLMs usually requires multi-dimensional rubrics to adequately assess quality and guide the improvement of reinforcement learning. However, a critical dilemma inherent in this training paradigm is the imbalanced reward polarization along different rubric dimensions. Under this bottleneck, even if LLMs achieve relatively high rewards after training, they may still exhibit severe deficiencies in certain dimensions, leading to a direct deterioration in user experience. To address this problem, we propose Focal Reward, a novel objective to automatically balance the training of reinforcement learning under rubric-based rewards. Specifically, we first leverage an inverse reward projection mechanism to estimate the saturation degree of each criterion in the rubric, which forms the basis to calibrate the reward direction. Then, the final objective is designed with an automatically reweighting coefficient for each criterion to achieve the fine-grained balancing. Extensive experiments across three model scales and six benchmarks demonstrate that our Focal Reward method outperforms the strongest static aggregation baseline in all 18 model-benchmark comparisons. Rollout, mechanism, and ablation analyses further show that these gains arise from online, saturation-aware reallocation toward rubrics that still have room for improvement.

### [147] [On the Error-Correcting Effects of Stochasticity in Discrete Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26582)
*William Yuan,Sungwon Jeong,Amirali Aghazadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入分析了离散扩散模型中随机性对采样效率的影响，提出了一种名为DCRS的算法，通过引入受控随机性实现高效采样，在大幅提升推理速度的同时保持了高质量的生成结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离散扩散模型在生成任务中虽然表现出色，但推理速度较慢，且在采样效率与样本质量之间存在难以调和的矛盾。研究者旨在探究马尔可夫转移中的“随机性程度”如何影响采样权衡，并寻找一种能改善该权衡的机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为“离散搅动与重采样”（Discrete Churn and Restart Sampling, DCRS）的新型推理算法。该方法通过在离散扩散过程的逆向采样中交替进行前向与反向步骤，人为注入受控的随机性，利用冗余转移带来的误差校正机制来弥补确定性采样中的累积误差。

Result: 在合成数据集和大规模基准测试中，DCRS算法在低采样步数下显著提升了速度与质量的权衡。在图像生成任务中，该方法能在保持样本质量的前提下，将采样步数减少至原来的十分之一。在语言建模任务中，其效果则受限于具体的损坏过程和采样流程。

Conclusion: 研究证明了通过在离散扩散模型的采样过程中引入受控的随机性（即DCRS算法），可以有效平衡采样效率与样本质量，从而在较少的采样步数下实现高质量的生成。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models achieve strong performance in text and image generation, but their inference remains slow and must inherently balance sampling efficiency and sample quality. In this work, we present a systematic study of how the \emph{degree of stochasticity} in Markov transitions governs the sampling tradeoff. We show that highly deterministic transitions converge rapidly but suffer from error accumulation, while more stochastic transitions converge more slowly yet can achieve higher final sample quality. Using an information-theoretic analysis, we identify the underlying mechanism as an error-correcting effect induced by \emph{redundant transitions} that symmetrically exchange mass between states, and show that these transitions can provably contract sampling errors. Motivated by this analysis, we propose \emph{Discrete Churn and Restart Sampling} (DCRS), a novel inference algorithm that injects controlled stochasticity by alternating between forward and reverse diffusion processes. Experiments on synthetic datasets and large-scale benchmarks show that DCRS improves the speed-quality tradeoff in the low number of function evaluations regime. On image datasets, DCRS achieves up to a $10\times$ reduction in sampling steps compared to standard samplers while maintaining competitive sample quality, whereas on language benchmarks, we observe more nuanced behavior depending on the corruption process and sampling procedure.
