### [148] [Near-Optimal Regret in Adversarial Kernel Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26585)
*Yu-Jie Zhang,Hao Qiu,Jonathan Scarlett,Kevin Jamieson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对对抗性核赌博机问题，提出了一种基于正则化偏差修正的指数权重算法，在一般核函数条件下实现了与随机环境下的最优遗憾一致的性能，并显著提升了Matérn核的分析界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决现有对抗性核赌博机算法在处理非随机损失函数时的局限性，特别是针对高维或连续空间的核函数（如Matérn核），旨在克服以往研究对特定假设（如秩一对抗）的依赖，并缩小与随机核赌博机最优遗憾界限之间的差距。

Method: 提出了一种基于指数权重（Exponential-weights）的算法，该算法结合了正则化的重要性加权损失估计器，并引入了一项显式的修正项来抵消正则化引入的偏差，从而有效地控制了由于核空间复杂性带来的遗憾增长。

Result: 证明了算法的遗憾界限为 $\widetilde{O}\big(\sqrt{T\, d_*(λ)\,\log|{X}|}\big)$；针对Matérn核，将遗憾界限提升至 $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{(ν+d)/(2ν+d)}\big)$，改进了先前的最优结果，并达到了该问题的最优速率。

Conclusion: 本研究成功为对抗性核赌博机问题提供了一个在正则化偏差修正下达到最优遗憾界限的算法，不仅消除了对随机环境或特定假设的依赖，还统一了对抗性与随机性核赌博机在复杂性度量下的理论界限。

Abstract: We study the adversarial kernel bandit problem, in which the loss at each round is induced by an arbitrary bounded element of a reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS). We propose an exponential-weights algorithm built on a regularized importance-weighted loss estimator, together with an explicit correction term that cancels the bias introduced by the regularization. Our main result bounds the regret by $\widetilde{O}\big(\sqrt{T\, d_*(λ)\,\log|{X}|}\big)$, where $d_*(λ)$ is a widely-adopted notion of effective dimension that captures the complexity of the kernel. Up to logarithmic factors, this matches the known rate achieved in the related stochastic kernel bandit problem. A notable application is the Matérn$(ν,d)$ kernel with smoothness parameter $ν$ on $\mathbb{R}^d$, for which our bound specializes to $\widetilde{O}\big(T^{(ν+d)/(2ν+d)}\big)$, improving over the best-known prior rate of Chatterji et al. [2019] while simultaneously removing the rank-one adversary assumption required by their analysis. Moreover, this rate is the same as the known optimal rate for stochastic kernel bandits, and also matches a lower bound from concurrent work up to a $\log T$ factor.

  Performance in childhood anemia prediction is driven more by population variation than model choice. TabPFN provides advantages in low-resource settings through improved discrimination and calibration, highlighting foundation models as promising tools for data-scarce global health prediction.

### [150] [Spend Your Rollouts Where It Counts: Rollout Allocation for Group-Based RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26606)
*Woojeong Kim,Ziyi Yang,Jing Nathan Yan,Jialu Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Pilot-Commit 是一种用于大模型强化学习的高效计算分配框架，通过先评估再分配的方式，将计算资源集中在能提供高学习信号的提示词上，从而显著提升了训练效率和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在基于群组的强化学习（RL）中，为所有提示词（prompt）分配等量的计算资源会导致大量算力浪费在奖励分布已收敛的提示词上。为了提高训练效率，需要一种在线机制来动态识别并优先处理具有高学习潜力（高奖励方差）的提示词。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Pilot-Commit”的预算感知滚动分配框架。该方法将 prompt 评估与策略优化解耦，首先通过“试点（Pilot）”阶段利用少量计算预算估算 prompt 的信息量，随后将剩余的大部分计算资源（“承诺（Commit）”）集中分配给具有高学习价值（即奖励方差大）的 prompt，并跳过低信号的 prompt。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试中，Pilot-Commit 在保持模型性能的同时，大幅降低了采样成本。在 1.5B 到 14B 参数模型规模下，其达到目标准确率的速度比 GRPO 快 1.9 倍，比 DAPO 快 4.0 倍。

Conclusion: Pilot-Commit 通过在线的“试点-承诺”机制成功解决了强化学习中计算资源分配不均的问题，证明了根据 prompt 的信息增益动态分配计算预算能够显著提升大模型后训练的效率。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is the dominant paradigm for post-training large language models. However, in the online, on-policy setting, rollout generation dominates the computational cost of training. Group-based policy optimization methods compute advantages from multiple rollouts per prompt, yet they indiscriminately allocate budget to prompts with collapsed reward distributions, wasting expensive rollouts on negligible learning signals. We demonstrate that group-based updates are most effective in regimes of high reward variance. Since the policy evolves throughout training, prompt informativeness must be estimated online rather than precomputed, but exhaustively evaluating every prompt is computationally prohibitive. We introduce Pilot-Commit, a budget-aware rollout allocation framework for group-based RL post-training. Pilot-Commit decouples prompt evaluation from exploitation: a pilot stage estimates per-prompt informativeness using a fraction of the budget, and the remaining rollouts are allocated to high-leverage prompts while low-signal prompts are skipped. Across multiple math reasoning benchmarks and model scales from 1.5B to 14B parameters, Pilot-Commit matches baseline accuracy with significantly lower sampling costs, reaching target accuracy up to $1.9\times$ faster than GRPO and $4.0\times$ faster than DAPO in cumulative rollouts.

### [151] [PIDM-DP: Physics-Informed Diffusion with Dormand-Prince Integration for Chaotic System Identification and State Reconstruction across Multiple Dynamical Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26619)
*Shailendra Dabral*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将5阶Dormand-Prince ODE积分器深度融合于扩散模型的物理信息重构框架（PIDM-DP），通过线性调度引导机制有效解决了刚性混沌系统的轨迹重构难题，实现了比传统方法（如EnKF）更高的精度与动力学一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌动力系统在稀疏和噪声观测下的连续状态轨迹重构是动力学领域的核心难题。现有的物理信息方法在处理复杂、高维或具有刚性特征的混沌系统时，往往因梯度不稳定性或模型拟合不足而表现欠佳，需要一种能够平衡数据驱动模型灵活性与物理规律严谨性的新方法。

Method: 提出了“物理信息扩散模型与Dormand-Prince积分器（PIDM-DP）”：1. 将5阶Dormand-Prince（DP-RK45）ODE积分器嵌入DDPM的反向采样循环；2. 利用自动微分在每个去噪步骤反向传播物理残差，以确保轨迹满足系统方程；3. 采用物理权重线性调度机制（Linear-scheduled guidance），有效缓解了高噪声下的梯度爆炸问题。

Result: 在Lorenz、Rössler、5D超混沌、20D Lorenz-96及Rabinovich-Fabrikant等五个基准系统中表现优异。相比无约束扩散基线，重构RMSE最高提升了15.4倍；在处理刚性系统时，显著优于集合卡尔曼滤波（EnKF）；在分布外（OOD）测试中，RMSE达到了0.1097，验证了模型在极端条件下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PIDM-DP 证明了通过将物理约束（ODE积分器）直接嵌入扩散模型的去噪过程，可以有效解决混沌动力系统在稀疏、噪声观测下的轨迹重构难题。该方法不仅在精度上显著优于基准模型，且在拓扑性质上有效保留了混沌系统的动力学特征，特别是在处理刚性（stiff）系统时表现出卓越的稳健性。

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous state trajectories of chaotic dynamical systems from sparse, noisy observations remains a fundamental open problem in nonlinear science. We introduce the Physics-Informed Diffusion Model with Dormand-Prince Integration (PIDM-DP), which embeds a fully differentiable 5th-order Dormand-Prince (DP-RK45) ODE integrator directly into the reverse sampling loop of a Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model (DDPM). At each denoising step, physics residuals are back-propagated via automatic differentiation, constraining every generated trajectory to satisfy the system's governing equations to 5th-order accuracy. A linear-scheduled guidance mechanism that ramps the physics weight from zero at high noise levels to its full value near the clean-data limit prevents the gradient explosions that cause naive physics-informed approaches to fail on stiff systems with Jacobian eigenvalues of order $O(10^3)$. Evaluated across five benchmark systems of increasing complexity 3D Lorenz, 3D Rössler, 5D Hyperchaotic, 20D Lorenz-96, and the stiff 3D Rabinovich-Fabrikant at 10% observation density with additive Gaussian noise ($σ=0.05$), PIDM-DP achieves reconstruction RMSE improvements of up to $15.4\times$ over an unconstrained diffusion baseline and decisively outperforms the Ensemble Kalman Filter on stiff systems where ensemble covariance collapses. On the Rabinovich-Fabrikant out-of-distribution benchmark, PIDM-DP attains RMSE $0.1097 \pm 0.0269$ versus $0.9443 \pm 0.5288$ (unconstrained diffusion, $8.6\times$ worse) and $0.3561 \pm 0.3040$ (EnKF, $3.2\times$ worse), with $p<0.001$ in paired Wilcoxon tests ($N = 30$). Topological validation via the Rosenstein Lyapunov estimator confirms that PIDM-DP preserves the chaotic invariant measure.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 RT-Lynx 框架，核心方法包括：1. 针对激活值而非权重进行 N:M 半结构化稀疏化；2. 引入误差补偿技术以减少因稀疏化导致的生成质量损失；3. 开发针对该稀疏模式高度优化的 CUDA 内核以实现硬件层面的加速。

Result: 实验结果表明，RT-Lynx 在保持原模型生成质量的同时，在多个扩散模型上实现了线性层平均高达 1.55 倍的推理速度提升。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将稀疏化重点从权重转移至激活值，证明了利用激活值的稀疏性进行 N:M 半结构化加速是提升扩散 Transformer 推理效率的有效路径，为模型压缩领域提供了新的研究范式。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiT) achieve strong performance in image generation but incur substantial inference costs. While prior work has reduced this cost via quantization and distillation, semi-structured sparsity, which can nearly halve FLOPs, remains underexplored. A key reason is that most existing approaches focus on weight sparsification, and pruning 50% of the weights can remove critical model capacity and degrade generation quality. Our study, however, shows that DiT activations are intrinsically sparse and significantly more robust to N:M semi-structured sparsification than weights. Motivated by this observation, we advocate a paradigm shift from weight sparsification to activation sparsification. We propose RT-Lynx, which applies N:M sparsification to activations and incorporates error-compensation techniques to mitigate accuracy loss. We further implement highly optimized CUDA kernels tailored to this setting, achieving up to a 1.55x speedup on average in linear layers. Extensive experiments across multiple diffusion models demonstrate that our method preserves the generation quality of the original models while substantially accelerating inference.

### [153] [More Expressive Feedforward Layers: Part I. Token-Adaptive Mixing of Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26647)
*Mingze Wang,Jinbo Wang,Yikuan Xia,Kai Shen,Shu Zhong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 模型中的 FFN 层普遍采用单一固定的激活函数（如 ReLU, SwiGLU），忽略了不同令牌可能需要不同非线性变换的需求，从而限制了模型的表达能力。因此，作者旨在探索一种更具灵活性和自适应性的激活机制。

Method: 1. 提出“激活混合”（MoA）：利用轻量级输入依赖门控，对激活函数字典进行加权混合；2. 提出“可学习激活”（LA）：作为 MoA 的输入无关变体，对激活函数进行线性组合；3. 理论分析：证明了固定激活函数 FFN、LA 和 MoA 之间在有限宽度下的表达能力存在严格的包含关系（MoA > LA > 固定激活）。

Result: 在 0.12B 到 2B 参数规模的密集模型和 MoE 模型上进行的预训练实验表明，MoA 相比基准模型能持续获得更低的最终损失值，并表现出更好的缩放（scaling）行为。

Conclusion: MoA 是一种简单且高效的机制，通过引入令牌自适应的激活函数混合，能够显著提升大语言模型中 FFN 的表达能力，且仅带来极小的额外参数和计算开销，是优化 Transformer 架构的有效方向。

Abstract: Feedforward network (FFN) layers account for a large fraction of parameters and nonlinear expressivity in Transformer-based large language models (LLMs). Despite the evolution from ReLU and GELU to gated variants such as SwiGLU, most FFN designs still use a single fixed activation function, applying the same nonlinear transformation to all tokens. In this work, we propose Mixture of Activations (MoA), a token-adaptive FFN design that mixes a dictionary of activation functions using lightweight input-dependent gates while sharing the same linear projections. As an input-independent counterpart, we also introduce learnable activations (LA), which form linear combinations of activation functions for both ReLU-type and SwiGLU-type FFNs. Theoretically, we establish strict finite-width expressive separations among fixed-activation FFNs, LA, and MoA: LA strictly contains fixed-activation FFNs, while MoA strictly contains LA, with the additional expressivity arising from input-dependent nonlinear hybridization. Empirically, we evaluate MoA through extensive pre-training experiments on dense and MoE language models ranging from 0.12B to 2B parameters under different token budgets, optimizers, and learning rate schedules. MoA consistently achieves lower terminal loss and exhibits more favorable scaling behavior than well-tuned baselines, with minimal parameter and computational overhead. These results suggest that token-adaptive activation mixing is a simple and effective mechanism for improving FFN expressivity in LLMs.

### [154] [Bilevel Optimization over Saddle Points of Zero-Sum Markov Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26654)
*Zihao Zheng,Irwin King,Songtao Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对双层强化学习中下层为多智能体博弈的问题，提出了PANDA算法，通过Nikaido-Isoda函数规避了二阶梯度计算，实现了在复杂竞争环境下的高效且理论最优的优化求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大多数双层强化学习方法仅限于单策略环境，无法处理诸如激励设计等涉及多策略交互的竞争性博弈结构。因此，作者旨在解决下层为正则化极小极大零和马尔可夫博弈的双层优化问题。

Method: 提出了一种基于惩罚函数的惩罚增强Nikaido-Isoda下降-上升（PANDA）算法，该方法利用Nikaido-Isoda函数将双层优化问题转化为单层求解，通过一阶策略梯度法避免了对高昂的二阶导数计算需求。

Result: 理论分析证明，PANDA算法在无需假设UL或LL目标函数凸性的情况下收敛至驻点；在迭代复杂度上达到 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-1})$，样本复杂度达到 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-3})$，与当前最先进的单策略双层强化学习方法持平，且实验验证了其优越性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的PANDA算法通过利用极小极大博弈结构，在不需要二阶导数信息或计算高阶超梯度的情况下，有效解决了双层强化学习中的竞争交互问题，并实现了理论上最优的收敛速率。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) often has a hierarchical structure, where an upper-level (UL) learner selects model parameters and a lower-level (LL) decision-making process responds, naturally leading to a bilevel optimization problem. Most existing bilevel RL methods assume a single-policy LL Markov decision process (MDP), and therefore fail to capture competitive structures arising in applications such as incentive design, where multiple policies interact. We study bilevel optimization problems in which the LL problem is a regularized min-max zero-sum Markov game and the UL objective is optimized through the saddle-point equilibrium induced by the LL game. In this work, we propose penalty-augmented Nikaido-Isoda descent-ascent (PANDA), a penalty-based first-order policy-gradient method based on the Nikaido-Isoda function. By exploiting the min-max game structure, PANDA avoids computing UL hypergradients and does not require second-order information. We prove that PANDA converges to stationary points without convexity assumptions on either the UL or LL objectives. Moreover, PANDA reaches an $ε$-stationary point in $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-1})$ iterations with sample complexity $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(ε^{-3})$, matching the best-known rates for bilevel RL with single-policy LL MDPs. Experiments demonstrate the superior performance of PANDA over closely related baselines.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在极低比特量化下性能衰减严重，而现有的训练后量化方法效果不佳，量化感知训练成本过高。此外，现有的混合精度策略多依赖于粗粒度或启发式的灵敏度分析，未能充分利用权重矩阵内部的细粒度变化。

Method: 提出了一种基于强化学习（PPO算法）的分配控制器。该方法以列块为单位进行细粒度位宽分配，并结合了激活感知校准、轻量级单元量化器拟合以及显式的有效比特核算，在全局存储预算约束下优化量化策略。

Abstract: Quantization is an effective approach to reduce the memory footprint and inference cost of large language models (LLMs), yet maintaining performance in the ultra-low-bit regime remains challenging. Existing post-training methods often suffer from severe accuracy degradation, while quantization-aware training requires costly retraining and additional resources. Moreover, most mixed-precision strategies rely on coarse-grained or heuristic sensitivity analysis that overlooks fine-grained variations within weight matrices. We propose WINDQuant, a reinforcement-learning-based allocation controller for ultra-low-bit LLM quantization. Rather than introducing another low-level quantization operator, WINDQuant learns how to assign bit-widths and quantization treatments to fine-grained column chunks under a global storage budget. By operating at the column-chunk level, WINDQuant enables flexible and fine-grained precision assignment within layers under a global target bit-width. The implementation combines PPO with activation-aware calibration, lightweight per-unit quantizer fitting, and explicit effective-bit accounting of the learned mixed-precision plan. Experiments on LLaMA models demonstrate that WINDQuant achieves competitive performance in ultra-low-bit settings while reducing optimization overhead relative to retraining-based approaches, highlighting reinforcement learning as a practical controller for adaptive mixed-precision quantization.

### [156] [Beyond Trajectory-Level Attribution: Graph-Based Credit Assignment for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26684)
*Xin Cheng,Shuo He,Lang Feng,HaiYang Xu,Ming Yan,Lei Feng,Bo An*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GraphGPO 是一种新型强化学习算法，它通过构建状态转移图并利用全局信息进行细粒度的步级信用分配，克服了传统方法仅依赖轨迹最终结果的局限，显著增强了大语言模型智能体的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于组的强化学习方法主要依赖粗粒度的轨迹级反馈，无法准确评估单步动作的贡献，导致在失败轨迹中仍有价值的步骤被忽略，限制了模型学习效率和性能。

Method: 提出基于图的组策略优化（GraphGPO）：首先将所有采样轨迹聚合为统一的状态转移图；其次，利用图中编码的全局信息估算每个状态距离任务目标的距离；最后，通过计算“基于图的优势（graph-based advantage）”来评估每一步转移对缩短目标距离的贡献，从而实现细粒度的信用分配。

Result: GraphGPO 显著提升了模型训练效率，并在多个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了最先进的（SOTA）性能。

Conclusion: GraphGPO 通过引入图结构来细化强化学习中的信用分配问题，有效解决了传统基于轨迹反馈方法在复杂任务中评估不准确的难题，为提升大语言模型智能体的训练效率和性能提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Group-based reinforcement learning (RL) methods have achieved remarkable success in improving the performance of large language models (LLMs) and have been rapidly extended to agentic tasks. However, their credit assignment relies heavily on coarse-grained trajectory-level attribution according to final outcomes, making it difficult to capture the contribution of individual steps, such as valuable steps obscured within failed trajectories. To uncover latent information and enable more faithful step-level credit assignment, we propose Graph-based Group Policy Optimization (GraphGPO), which first aggregates all rollout trajectories into a unified state-transition graph and then estimates the distance from each state to the task goal using the global information encoded in the graph. Finally, GraphGPO assigns credit to each edge by estimating a graph-based advantage, based on how much the transition reduces the distance to the task goal. In this way, GraphGPO significantly improves training efficiency and achieves state-of-the-art performance across a range of challenging benchmarks.

</details>

Abstract: Epidemic forecasting faces a fundamental challenge: human behavior dynamically responds to disease spread, creating feedback loops that induce distribution shifts at policy intervention points. This renders data-driven models unreliable under distribution shift. We propose \textbf{SL-BiLEM} (Structured Learnable Behavior-in-the-Loop Epidemic Model), leveraging physical constraints as regularization for robust extrapolation. The framework decomposes effective transmission as $β_{\text{eff}}(t,g) = β_0(g) \times m_{\text{policy}}(t) \times m_{\text{media}}(t) \times m_{\text{comp}}(t,g)$, where monotonicity, smoothness, and bounded-jump constraints on the learned compliance function maintain predictive validity under novel policy regimes. SL-BiLEM demonstrates: (1) 76\% improvement over neural-mechanistic baselines, with only 53\% OOD degradation versus 1142\% for neural baselines under policy-induced shift; (2) 100\% bootstrap CI coverage across 27 synthetic counterfactual experiments; and (3) Treatment Effect Accuracy exceeding 0.85. Abstract: Major data protection regulations all mention the "right to be forgotten," and that's what pushed federated unlearning (FU) techniques forward. But one stubborn issue remains: catastrophic forgetting--you erase the target knowledge, yet somehow you also end up throwing out essential retained knowledge, which then hurts the model's global generalization.
  To get a better balance between unlearning effectiveness and generalization ability, we propose something called Image Feature Fusion-based Federated Client Unlearning (IFF-FCU). The idea is to bring in a linear Image Feature Fusion mechanism (Mixup) that dynamically creates mixed samples, bridging the gap between forget-distribution and retain-distribution. What this strategy does isn't just deleting a few discrete data points--it theoretically widens and regularizes the forgetting boundary.

### [159] [MTL-FNO: A Lightweight Multi-Task Fourier Neural Operator for Sparse Field Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26718)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于硬参数共享的多任务傅里叶神经算子（MTL-FNO）框架：1. 将参数划分为共享组件和低秩任务特定组件以实现模型压缩；2. 采用极坐标分解对谱权重进行解耦，将幅度和相位分离以缓解任务冲突；3. 引入凯莱变换（Cayley transform）将约束优化问题转化为无约束优化，确保训练过程中的酉几何保真度。

Abstract: Efficient onboard multi-field sparse reconstruction is essential for the autonomous operation of aerospace vehicles. While existing deep learning models exhibit promise for single-field reconstruction, deploying multiple independent models leads to prohibitive model size growth and fails to exploit cross-field correlations, particularly under few-shot conditions. To address these challenges, we first propose a lightweight multi-task Fourier neural operator (MTL-FNO), an end-to-end joint training framework based on hard parameter sharing. In each layer, the parameters are divided into shared and task-specific components to capture common features across fields while preserving task-specific characteristics. Moreover, the task-specific fine-tuning parameters are implemented as low-rank terms, achieving substantial model compression. Second, to address the difficulty of co-optimizing shared and task-specific parameters along with their real and imaginary parts, we revisit the FNO's spectral weight from a polar-form perspective and devise a physically meaningful decoupled optimization scheme. Specifically, we apply polar decomposition to slice-wise disentangle the spectral weight into a unitary tensor encoding phase information and a positive semi-definite tensor characterizing amplitude. By decoupling the optimization of phase and amplitude, our method can effectively mitigate tasks conflict. Meanwhile, to preserve unitary geometric fidelity during training, the Cayley transform is introduced to reparameterize the unitary tensor, converting the constrained optimization problem to an unconstrained one. Finally, the effectiveness of the proposed method under few-shot conditions is validated on two representative engineering cases. Results show that MTL-FNO achieves accuracy comparable to or even surpassing that of standard FNO, while reducing total model size by 76% and 60%, respectively.

</details>


### [160] [APEX: Amplitude Anchors and Phase Priors for Target-Scarce Higher-Frequency Wave Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26732)
*Yifan Sun,Lei Cheng,Sijie Chen,Ting Zhang,Jianlong Li,Shikai Fang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对高频波场预测中相位信息易丢失且数据稀缺的问题，本文提出了一种 APEX 框架，通过提取低频振幅作为锚点并引入相位先验进行增强，实现了优于传统迁移学习方法的高频波场重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在波场预测中，高频数据获取成本高昂，且跨频率迁移存在不对称性——低频的振幅结构相对稳定，而相位的振荡细节随频率增加迅速恶化。现有的神经算子难以在目标数据稀缺的情况下有效完成从低频到高频的直接外推。

Method: 提出了 APEX（Amplitude-anchored and Phase-prior-guided Enhancement）框架：首先利用低频神经算子在目标频率生成粗预测，并提取其中的振幅信息作为结构锚点；随后利用条件流匹配（Conditional Flow-matching）增强器，结合受格林函数启发的相位先验，重建高频波场。

Result: 在 SimpleWave、Helmholtz 和 Maxwell 等基准测试中，APEX 在极少量的目标频率监督下，性能显著优于直接外推、目标自适应算子及联合生成式基准模型。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，针对振荡波场的可靠高频预测不应依赖全复场域的直接端到端迁移，而应采用“重用可迁移的粗粒度结构+分别恢复缺失的振荡细节”的解耦策略，从而有效解决跨频率预测中的相位退化难题。

Abstract: Learning-based surrogates have become increasingly effective for wave-field prediction, and neural operators in particular have shown strong performance within observed frequency regimes. However, higher-frequency prediction under scarce target supervision remains comparatively underexplored, especially in wave problems where higher-frequency data are substantially more expensive to simulate or measure than lower-frequency data. A central difficulty is that cross-frequency transfer is inherently asymmetric: coarse amplitude structure remains relatively stable across frequencies, whereas phase-sensitive oscillatory structure deteriorates much more rapidly as frequency increases. Motivated by this asymmetry, we propose APEX, Amplitude-anchored and Phase-prior-guided Enhancement from eXtrapolated coarse predictions, a framework for target-scarce higher-frequency wave-field prediction. A lower-frequency neural operator first provides a coarse prediction in the target-frequency regime, from which we retain only the amplitude as a transferable structural anchor. A conditional flow-matching enhancer then reconstructs the target higher-frequency field under the guidance of a Green's-function-inspired phase prior. Experiments on SimpleWave, Helmholtz, and Maxwell benchmarks show that APEX consistently outperforms direct lower-to-higher extrapolation, target-adapted operator, and joint generative baselines under limited target-frequency supervision. Our results suggest that reliable higher-frequency prediction of oscillatory wave fields should not rely on direct end-to-end transfer of the full complex field, but instead on explicitly reusing transferable coarse structure while separately recovering the missing oscillatory detail.

### [161] [Stabilizing Recurrent Dynamics for Test-Time Scalable Latent Reasoning in Looped Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26733)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的循环语言模型（LoopLMs）在增加推理深度时存在性能崩溃问题，缺乏可靠的测试时扩展能力。作者认为这是因为模型在有效性与稳定性之间缺乏权衡，将推理过程视作不确定性降低的过程，提出通过追求稳定的不动点来提升模型表现。

Method: 提出STARS（稳定性驱动的循环扩展）训练框架，核心在于引入雅可比谱半径正则化（Jacobian Spectral Radius Regularization）并结合随机循环采样，通过数学约束将模型的潜在状态引导至渐近稳定的不动点。

Result: 在算术任务上实现了可靠的测试时扩展；在复杂数学推理任务中，STARS有效缓解了深度增加导致的性能退化问题，并提升了模型推理的峰值性能。

Conclusion: STARS通过正则化手段强制循环语言模型的潜在状态趋向于稳定的不动点，成功解决了模型在推理深度增加时性能崩溃的问题，实现了可靠的测试时扩展（test-time scaling）。

Abstract: Looped Language Models (LoopLMs) enable efficient latent reasoning through depth recurrence, yet exhibit unreliable test-time scaling behavior: performance often peaks at a certain iteration depth and then collapses with further recurrence. Through latent dynamics analysis, we find an inherent trade-off between stability and effectiveness in existing architectures and strategies. By conceptualizing reasoning as uncertainty reduction, we propose that convergence toward stable fixed points while preserving effectiveness represents a promising way. To this end, we propose STARS (STAbility-driven Recurrent Scaling), a training framework that constrains latent states to approach asymptotically stable fixed points. This is realized via efficient Jacobian Spectral Radius Regularization with random loop sampling, enabling STARS to maximize effectiveness while ensuring rigorous stability. Experiments on arithmetic tasks show that STARS achieves reliable test-time scaling, and on complex mathematical reasoning it substantially mitigates performance degradation as recurrence depth increases while also improving peak performance.

To model complex temporal causal dependencies, PTCD employs a dual-scale iterative attention mechanism to capture window-level causal relationships, and a Gaussian mixture with a context-level routing mechanism to handle heterogeneous exogenous distributions. To further address distribution shifts across causal graphs, PTCD adopts a pretraining paradigm on synthetic datasets that integrates intervention-based learning and a causal mixup strategy, promoting stable causal discovery and stronger generalization. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world out-of-distribution (OOD) datasets demonstrate that PTCD excels in both causal discovery and root cause identification.

### [163] [Ratio-Variance Regularized Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26784)
*Yu Luo,Shuo Han,Yihan Hu,Lei Lv,Huaping Liu,Fuchun Sun,Jianye Hao,Dong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: R²VPO 提出了一种用策略比率方差正则化代替启发式剪切的新型强化学习优化方法，通过更智能的“软刹车”机制，显著提升了 LLM 推理任务和机器人控制中的性能与样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的同策略强化学习（如 PPO）过度依赖启发式剪切（clipping）来强制实施信任域，这会导致算法无差别地截断那些具有高回报但高发散性的更新，从而浪费了宝贵的梯度信号并限制了训练效率。

Method: 提出了“比率方差正则化策略优化”（R²VPO）。该方法通过引入基于原始-对偶优化框架的约束来显式限制策略比率的方差，替代了 PPO 中传统的启发式剪切机制，起到“软刹车”的作用，从而平衡了更新幅度和策略稳定性。

Result: 在 7 种不同规模的大语言模型（涵盖快、慢推理范式）和 10 项机器人控制任务上的测试表明，R²VPO 在数学推理基准测试中显著提升了性能（尤其在小模型上），并提高了样本效率；在连续控制领域，其性能也持续优于 PPO 基准，尤其是在稀疏奖励和动态环境中表现出色。

Conclusion: 通过对策略比率方差进行正则化，R²VPO 提供了一种替代启发式剪切的原则性方法，能够在保持训练稳定性的同时最大化梯度信息的利用，为策略优化提供了一个更通用且高效的框架。

Abstract: Standard on-policy reinforcement learning relies on heuristic clipping to enforce trust regions, but this mechanism imposes a severe cost by indiscriminately truncating high-return yet high-divergence updates. We demonstrate that explicitly constraining the policy ratio variance provides a principled local approximation to trust-region constraints, eliminating the need for binary hard clipping. By acting as a distributional ``soft brake'', this approach preserves critical gradient signals from novel discoveries while naturally down-weighting and enabling the reuse of stale, off-policy data. We introduce ${\bf R}^2{\bf VPO}$ (Ratio-Variance Regularized Policy Optimization), which implements this constraint via a primal-dual optimization framework. Extensive evaluations across $7$ LLM scales, spanning both fast and slow reasoning paradigms, and $10$ robotic control tasks demonstrate the generality of the proposed approach. R$^2$VPO achieves substantial performance gains on mathematical reasoning benchmarks, with particularly pronounced improvements on smaller models, while significantly improving sample efficiency. Furthermore, it consistently outperforms PPO baselines in continuous control domains, particularly in sparse-reward and dynamic environments. Together, these findings establish ratio-variance regularization as a principled foundation for stable and data-efficient policy optimization.

### [164] [PATE-TabTransGAN: Differentially Private Synthetic Tabular Data Generation via Transformer-Based Student Discrimination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26802)
*M. Youssef,M. Woźniak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PATE-TabTransGAN 结合了 Transformer 模型与 PATE 隐私机制，在实现形式化差分隐私保障的同时，显著提升了合成表格数据的质量和特征依赖建模能力，在多项基准测试中优于现有的差分隐私合成方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在差分隐私（DP）框架下生成高保真的合成表格数据是一个悬而未决的挑战。现有的方法往往在“严格的理论隐私保障”与“捕捉复杂特征依赖的建模能力”之间难以兼顾：强隐私方法通常导致数据质量受损，而高保真生成模型往往仅提供经验性的隐私保护。该研究旨在提出一种既能提供形式化隐私保证，又能精准建模特征依赖的框架。

Method: 1. 采用 PATE（教师集成隐私聚合）框架，利用多个在不相交数据集上训练的逻辑回归教师模型进行投票。
2. 使用 Transformer 架构作为学生判别器，以增强对表格数据复杂列间依赖关系的捕捉能力。
3. 引入 GNMax RDP 审计机制进行隐私成本管理，确保提供严格的 (ε, δ)-差分隐私保证。
4. 训练残差生成器对抗该学生判别器，通过后处理机制继承隐私保证。

Result: 在四个基准数据集（Adult, Breast, Cardio, Cervical）上的实验表明，PATE-TabTransGAN 在 AUROC 指标上达到了最优或并列最优；在 AUCPR 指标上，该方法在多个数据集上超越或匹配了现有的 SOTA 方法（如 PATE-GAN、DP-GAN、DP-CTGAN），并澄清了在 Adult 数据集上表现差异源于评估范式的不同而非模型本身的缺陷。

Conclusion: PATE-TabTransGAN 成功结合了 PATE 的形式化差分隐私保护与 Transformer 在捕捉复杂特征依赖方面的强大建模能力，证明了在保留数据效用的同时实现严格的隐私保障是可行的。该研究为生成式模型在隐私敏感的表格数据合成领域提供了强有力的架构选择。

Abstract: Generating high-fidelity synthetic tabular data under formal differential privacy guarantees remains an open challenge. Methods that provide strong theoretical protection typically sacrifice the modeling of inter-feature dependencies required for realistic synthesis, while architectures that excel at capturing complex column relationships offer only empirical privacy guarantees. We present PATE-TabTransGAN, a generative framework that integrates the Private Aggregation of Teacher Ensembles (PATE) mechanism with a Transformer-based student discriminator to jointly address both requirements, and employs a GNMax RDP accountant for numerically stable privacy accounting. An ensemble of Logistic Regression teachers trained on disjoint partitions supervise the student via noisy-aggregated labels, and a residual generator is optimized against this differentially private student, inheriting formal (ε, δ)-DP guarantees by post-processing. PATE-TabTransGAN was compared with PATE-GAN, DP-GAN, and DP-CTGAN, considered state-of-the-art in differentially private tabular synthesis. Experiments conducted on four tabular benchmarks (Adult, Breast, Cardio, Cervical) confirmed the high quality of the proposed method: PATE-TabTransGAN attains the best or tied-best AUROC on all four datasets. On AUCPR it matches the strongest baseline on Cardio, leads on Cervical, and trails on Breast; on Adult, we demonstrate that AUCPR is highly sensitive to positive-class convention, and that the observed gap is consistent with a convention difference between evaluation pipelines rather than a synthesis deficit.

### [165] [Innovation: An Almost Characterization of Hallucination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26808)
*Nishant P. Das,Piyush Srivastava*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了大型语言模型产生幻觉的根本原因是其固有的“创新性”（即输出训练集之外内容的倾向），证明了幻觉在统计上是不可避免的，即使放弃模型校准也无法根除，并提供了基于“缺失质量”的更精确的幻觉率下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型（LLM）中幻觉问题的本质，特别是回答以下两个关键问题：一是校准后的 LLM 为何必然产生幻觉；二是放弃模型校准是否可以彻底消除幻觉。

Method: 通过引入“创新性（Innovation）”这一新属性（定义为模型产生训练数据之外输出的倾向），将其与 Kalai 和 Vempala 提出的幻觉条件进行数学关联，利用概率论证分析创新性、校准（Calibration）与幻觉之间的内在联系，并推导出基于创新率的幻觉下界。

Result: 证明了创新性是幻觉的近乎充分必要条件，即幻觉暗示了创新性，反之亦然；确立了基于创新率的幻觉下界，并证明了即便不进行校准，幻觉依然随模型对训练数据的“缺失质量（Missing Mass）”而存在。

Conclusion: 创新性（Innovation）是导致幻觉的核心原因。即使放弃模型校准，幻觉也是不可避免的，因为创新性与幻觉之间存在近乎等价的关系。研究通过建立创新率与缺失质量之间的联系，进一步完善并拓宽了大型语言模型幻觉率的理论下界。

Abstract: Hallucination is a central limitation of large language models (LLMs), and substantial effort has been devoted to understanding and mitigating it. Towards this, Kalai and Vempala (STOC 2024) introduced a probabilistic framework formalizing calibration and hallucination, and showed that, with high probability, calibrated LLMs hallucinate roughly at the rate of the "missing mass", a measure of how incomplete the training data is relative to its source. This raises two fundamental questions: (i) what property of a calibrated LLM makes hallucinations unavoidable? and (ii) can hallucinations be avoided by giving up calibration? We answer these questions by introducing a simpler property we call innovation that measures the tendency of a model to produce outputs outside the training data. We show that innovation is implied by the condition for hallucination identified by Kalai and Vempala, and, further, that it is an almost characterization of hallucination: hallucination implies innovation, and conversely, innovation implies hallucination with high probability. We also provide lower bounds on the hallucination rate based on the "innovation rate", and by relating innovation rate back to missing mass, we obtain new hallucination rate lower bounds based on missing mass that extend the results of Kalai and Vempala.

### [166] [The Kalman Evolve: Closing the Gap in Kalman Filtering via Interpretable Algorithm Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26830)
*Vasileios Saketos,Ming Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统卡尔曼滤波在非线性环境下的性能瓶颈，研究者利用大模型自动优化滤波器的更新结构，在保持递归特性的同时，显著提升了状态估计精度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出名为“Kalman Evolve”的框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）作为程序空间的结构化先验，在保持卡尔曼滤波递归形式的前提下，自动发现并生成非仿射的更新结构，同时联合优化噪声协方差参数。

Result: 在多普勒雷达、激光雷达定位及行人追踪等多种合成及真实数据集上，Kalman Evolve 均优于优化后的传统卡尔曼滤波（Optimized Kalman Filter），在均方根误差（RMSE）方面实现了最高 12% 的降低。

Abstract: State estimation is a fundamental problem in control and signal processing, for which the Kalman Filter provides an optimal solution under linear dynamics, Gaussian noise, and known noise covariances. However, these assumptions often fail in realistic sensing settings such as Doppler radar and LiDAR. In these cases, the optimal estimator is inherently nonlinear, which leads to systematic performance degradation. This creates a performance gap that cannot be eliminated by tuning the noise covariance parameters (i.e., the process and measurement noise in the Kalman Filter) alone. To address this limitation, we propose Kalman Evolve, a framework for discovering improved filtering algorithms by jointly optimizing both noise parameters and the update structure. Our approach leverages large language models (LLMs) as a structured prior over program space, enabling the generation of interpretable, non-affine modifications to the classical Kalman filter while preserving its recursive form. We provide analytical results establishing the suboptimality of affine estimators under common nonlinear sensing models, motivating the need for structure-aware updates. Across a range of synthetic and real-world tracking benchmarks, including Doppler radar, LiDAR-based localization, and pedestrian tracking, the discovered algorithms consistently improve over strong baselines such as the Optimized Kalman Filter, achieving up to 12\% reduction in RMSE. These results suggest that optimizing the structure of the Kalman filter, rather than only its parameters, provides a practical and interpretable way to improve state estimation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 MONA 优化器，在 Muon 的梯度处理流水线中引入了一个基于梯度差指数移动平均（EMA）的加速项。该方法通过将曲率感知机制与矩阵正交化相结合，在保持谱范数正则化的同时，实现了对优化方向的有效调节。

Result: 在 1B 到 68B 参数规模的 MoE 模型预训练中，MONA 的收敛速度和下游任务表现均优于 Muon 和 AdamW。特别是在 68B 规模模型及 1 万亿 token 的训练中，MONA 表现出色；在监督微调阶段，该模型在通用能力、数学推理和代码生成基准测试中均达到了 SOTA 水平。

Conclusion: MONA 成功地将曲率感知加速机制整合进 Muon 的矩阵正交化框架中，不仅保留了 Muon 的正则化优势，还显著增强了优化器跳出尖锐局部极小值的能力，为大规模 MoE 模型训练提供了一种更高效、稳健的优化方案。

Abstract: The Muon optimizer has recently offered a promising alternative to AdamW for large language model training, leveraging matrix orthogonalization to produce geometry-aware updates. However, like all first-order methods, Muon can become trapped in sharp local minima. In this work, we present MONA, an optimizer that bridges Muon's orthogonalization framework with curvature-aware acceleration. MONA adds an acceleration term directly into Muon's gradient processing pipeline. This term is calculated from the exponential moving average of gradient differences. We provide a detailed convergence analysis for MONA, showing that the acceleration term enables escape from sharp minima while preserving Muon's spectral-norm regularization. Empirically, MONA achieves better convergence and downstream task performance compared to both Muon and AdamW across three scales of Mixture-of-Experts pretraining, spanning from 1B to 68B parameters, with the largest model trained on 1 trillion tokens. Furthermore, we conduct supervised fine-tuning on the MOE-68B-A3B model and evaluate it on general capability, mathematical reasoning, and code generation benchmarks, where MONA achieves SOTA performance.

### [168] [Not All Disagreement Is Learnable: Token Teachability in On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26844)
*Yuanyi Wang,Su Lu,Yanggan Gu,Pengkai Wang,Yifan Yang,Zhaoyi Yan,Congkai Xie,Jianmin Wu,Hongxia Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了“可教性（Teachability）”概念，用于量化教师信号在特定上下文中的可学习性；据此开发了 TA-OPD（可教性感知策略蒸馏）方法，通过筛选高可教性位置的代币进行训练，无需额外的奖励模型或验证器。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5 和 Qwen3 的实验中，TA-OPD 在仅使用 5% 的保留代币的情况下，性能往往超过了全量代币的蒸馏，并且在效果上显著优于基于熵和散度的传统基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究重新定义了选择性策略蒸馏的核心逻辑：成功的蒸馏不仅依赖于选择显著性高的代币，更依赖于识别那些教师模型能够提供“可学习”修正信息的“可教性”代币。通过过滤掉学生模型难以吸收的噪声信号，TA-OPD 实现了更高的训练效率和性能表现。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student on its own rollouts with token-level teacher supervision. Recent selective OPD methods exploit the non-uniformity of OPD signals by prioritizing high-entropy or high-disagreement tokens. We revisit this principle and ask: which token-level teacher signals are actually learnable? Using a fixed-context diagnostic that measures same-context teacher-student KL reduction, we show that raw KL disagreement is a coarse proxy for learning value. It conflates learnable disagreement, where the teacher assigns corrective mass to the student's top-K candidates, with incompatible disagreement, where the teacher places mass mostly off the student's current support. We formalize this local compatibility as token teachability and show that it better predicts fixed-context improvement than raw KL alone. Motivated by this finding, we propose Teachability-Aware OPD (TA-OPD), a lightweight token-position selection method that applies OPD loss to high-teachability positions without reward models or verifiers. Across Qwen2.5 and Qwen 3 teacher-student settings, TA-OPD often surpasses full-token OPD with only 5% retained tokens and improves over entropy- and divergence-based baselines. Our results reframe selective OPD as selecting learnable teacher signals rather than merely salient tokens.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于能量的扩散模型（如去噪得分匹配）通常通过在不同噪声水平下破坏数据样本来学习能量，但这些方法分别侧重于空间差异或时间差异，存在明显的失效模式（failure modes）。因此，研究者旨在开发一种更有效的训练框架。

Method: 作者提出了时空噪声对比估计（stNCE）框架。该方法不再单一依赖空间或时间上的差异来学习能量函数，而是通过联合时空差异（joint spatiotemporal differences）来训练模型，从而统一并改进了现有的扩散模型训练目标。

Result: 实验结果表明，stNCE 在图像和分子密度估计任务中表现出与当前最先进方法相当甚至更好的性能，证明了该方法在学习复杂数据分布方面的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: stNCE 通过联合时空差异学习能量，成功克服了现有方法在空间或时间维度上的局限性，提供了一种更稳健、更统一的能量模型训练框架，并在图像和分子建模任务中展现了优异的性能。

Abstract: Learning an energy-based model from data samples is a central problem in machine learning. Many recent and popular methods, such as denoising score matching for training energy-based diffusion models, use stochastic interpolants to corrupt data samples at different noise levels indexed by a time variable. This defines a joint density over both the data space and time, and most methods learn its energy through either spatial or temporal differences. We identify distinct failure modes for both of these approaches. To solve them, we propose Spatiotemporal Noise-Contrastive Estimation (stNCE), a framework for learning the energy through joint spatiotemporal differences. stNCE unifies many existing methods and leads to new training objectives. Experiments on images and molecules demonstrate performance competitive with state-of-the-art density estimation methods.

To address this limitation, we introduce ProMoS, the first unsupervised generalist GAD framework, which detects anomalies by modeling the abundant normality in unlabeled data. ### [171] [The Strongest Teacher Is Not Always the Best Teacher: Student-Centric Answer Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26872)
*Zhengyu Hu,Zheyuan Xiao,Linxin Song,Fengqing Jiang,Yutai Li,Zhengyu Chen,Zhihan Xiong,Yue Liu,Junhao Lin,Yao Su,Lijie Hu,Kaize Ding,Xiao Teng,Radha Poovendran*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的LLM训练往往盲目依赖性能最强的教师模型来生成数据，假设“强教师即好老师”。作者指出这种假设在很多情况下并不成立，即使答案正确，强教师的思维路径或表达方式未必最适合特定阶段的学生模型，因此需要一种以学生为中心的数据选择机制。

Method: 提出了“以学生为中心的答案采样”（SCAS）框架。该方法受token级梯度分解启发，推导出了一个高效的、无需反向传播的预测指标，用于衡量特定学生学习某条数据时的“学习成本”，并以此为依据从多个教师生成的答案中筛选出最适合当前学生的数据。

Result: 在涵盖30个教师模型、6个学生基座模型和8项任务的广泛实验中，SCAS框架表现出持续的性能提升，验证了针对性匹配学生与教学数据的重要性。

Conclusion: 有效的知识蒸馏不应仅仅依赖教师模型的整体表现，而应优先考虑能够最小化特定学生模型学习成本的指导数据。SCAS框架证明了基于学生能力的自适应数据选择策略能显著提升蒸馏效果。

Abstract: LLM training increasingly relies on teacher-generated supervision, from synthetic responses to reasoning traces and tool-use demonstrations. Current practice often chooses the highest-performing teacher to generate student training data, implicitly treating teacher test performance as a proxy for teaching quality. We show that this assumption can fail: even when multiple teachers provide correct answers to the same question, the answer from the strongest teacher is not necessarily the best supervision for a given student. To address this gap, we propose Student-Centric Answer Sampling (SCAS), a framework that selects from verified teacher-generated answers according to their estimated student-centric learning cost. Motivated by a token-wise gradient decomposition, we derive an efficient forward-only proxy for this cost and use it to guide answer selection during training. Experiments across 30 teacher models, 6 student base models, and 8 tasks show that SCAS consistently improves student performance, suggesting that effective distillation should prioritize supervision matched to the current student rather than teacher strength alone.

### [172] [Negligible in Size, Significant in Effect: On Scale Vectors in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26895)
*Mingze Wang,Shuchen Zhu,Yuxin Fang,Binghui Li,Kai Shen,Shu Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统性地揭示了LLM中归一化层缩放向量的优化作用，指出其主要通过自放大效应提升训练稳定性。研究针对性地提出了三项轻量级改进措施，在多种模型规模下均能以微小成本显著降低预训练损失并优化缩放行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管缩放向量在现代大语言模型的归一化层中无处不在，但其背后的机制（如为何仅占极小参数量却对预训练至关重要）尚不清楚，缺乏系统的理论支撑与优化指导。

Method: 1. 理论分析：利用数学推导分析缩放向量对模型表达能力（Expressivity）和优化（Optimization）的影响；2. 实验验证：在0.12B至2B参数规模的稠密模型及混合专家模型（MoE）上进行大规模预训练实验；3. 机制研究：对比分析Input-Norm与Output-Norm层在权重衰减下的不同表现，并针对性提出改进策略。

Result: 1. 证实缩放向量通过对线性映射进行自放大预处理来改善优化，而非增加模型表达能力；2. 发现权重衰减对不同归一化层（Input-Norm与Output-Norm）的影响截然不同；3. 提出的改进策略在各种配置下均实现了更低的终止损失（terminal loss），并展现出更好的缩放性能，且几乎不增加计算与参数负担。

Conclusion: 通过对大语言模型（LLM）中归一化层缩放向量的深入分析，本文揭示了其在优化中的关键作用而非增加表达能力。提出的改进策略（分支异构性、布局优化、幅值方向重参数化）在多种规模模型和训练配置下均能以极低代价显著提升模型性能，为LLM架构设计提供了有效的优化指南。

Abstract: Normalization layers in modern large language models (LLMs) consist of a deterministic normalization operation and a learnable scale vector. While the normalization operation has been extensively studied, the scale vector remains poorly understood despite its ubiquitous use. In this work, we present a systematic study of scale vectors in LLMs from the perspectives of expressivity, optimization, and architectural structure. First, we show empirically that although scale vectors constitute only a negligible fraction of model parameters, removing them substantially degrades LLM pre-training. Our theory further shows that, in Pre-Norm architectures, scale vectors do not increase expressivity; instead, they improve optimization through a self-amplifying preconditioning effect on subsequent linear mappings. Second, we investigate the role of weight decay for scale vectors. By distinguishing Input-Norm and Output-Norm layers, we theoretically show that weight decay is beneficial for the former but harmful for the latter, due to their distinct roles in optimization and expressivity. Third, motivated by this understanding, we propose three lightweight and complementary improvements to scale vectors: branch-specific heterogeneity, improved placement around linear mappings, and magnitude-direction reparameterization. Both theory and experiments show that each improvement yields consistent gains. Finally, we combine these improvements into a unified scale-vector strategy and evaluate it through extensive LLM pre-training experiments on dense and mixture-of-experts models ranging from 0.12B to 2B parameters, across multiple optimizers and learning rate schedules, under industrial-scale token budgets. The unified strategy consistently achieves lower terminal loss than well-tuned baselines and exhibits more favorable scaling behavior, while adding negligible parameter and computational overhead.

### [173] [SPHERE-JEPA: Spherical Prediction with Homogeneous Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26900)
*Léo Nicollier,Max Dunitz,Marc Pic,Pablo Musé,Enric Meinhardt-Llopis,Gabriele Facciolo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了 SSL 中“高斯嵌入最优”的观点，证明了在黎曼流形上超球面均匀分布更具优势。为此提出了 SPHERE-JEPA 框架，通过强制实施超球面均匀分布显著提升了下游任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自监督学习（SSL）研究（如 LeJEPA）指出高斯嵌入在欧几里得空间中是最优的，但这一结论在低维流形（如超球面）上尚未得到验证。作者旨在探索流形约束下最优表示的几何特性，并解决高斯嵌入在处理流形数据时产生的偏差问题。

Method: 1. 通过极小化极大（minimax）分析，研究了在黎曼流形上 k-近邻（k-NN）和核岭回归（KRR）的最优几何表示。
2. 提出 SPHERE-JEPA 框架，将 LeJEPA 的 Cramer-Wold 投影机制调整为强制实施超球面均匀分布，而非高斯先验。

2. 实验表明，SPHERE-JEPA 在纹理检索任务中 mAP 提升超过 6%，在 ImageNet-1K (ViT-B/14) 上的线性探测性能提升了 1.8%。

Conclusion: 本文证明了黎曼流形上的均匀分布在下流任务中优于各向同性的高斯嵌入。研究揭示了高斯嵌入会导致各向异性邻域并产生偏差，而基于球面积分的 SPHERE-JEPA 框架能有效缓解这一问题，并在图像检索和分类任务中取得了显著性能提升。

Abstract: A fundamental open question in self-supervised learning (SSL) is the explicit characterization of the optimal geometry of the learned representations. Recently, LeJEPA identified isotropic Gaussian embeddings as optimal for minimizing downstream prediction risk in Euclidean spaces. However, the corresponding problem for distributions supported on lower-dimensional manifolds, such as the hypersphere, remains unexplored. In this work, we demonstrate that extending this minimax analysis to smooth distributions on Riemannian manifolds fundamentally changes the optimal solution. We show that, under a worst-case formulation, both k-nearest neighbors and kernel ridge regression induce hyperspherical uniformity. More precisely, we show that uniform distributions on manifolds are optimal for k-nearest neighbors, and that the uniform distribution on the sphere is optimal for kernel ridge regression with both the exponential dot-product kernel and the linear kernel. This theoretical insight reveals a fundamental limitation of Gaussian embeddings: their non-uniform density induces anisotropic k-NN neighborhoods, severely biasing the estimator. To correct this, we introduce SPHERE-JEPA, a theoretically grounded SSL framework. We adapt LeJEPA's Cram{é}r-Wold projection mechanism to enforce hyperspherical uniformity rather than a Gaussian prior. Empirically, SPHERE-JEPA yields significant improvements, boosting texture retrieval mAP by over 6%, while consistently matching or outperforming LeJEPA on standard benchmarks-including a +1.8% linear probing gain on ImageNet-1K (ViT-B/14).

### [174] [EEG-FM-Audit: A Systematic Evaluation and Analysis Pipeline for EEG Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26910)
*Xianheng Wang,Yige Yang,Damien Coyle*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了EEG-FM-Audit评估框架，通过严谨的基准测试、消融实验和生理特征探测，发现经过精心优化的监督学习基线在脑电分析中具有极强的竞争力，并揭示了现有脑电基础模型在特征利用和范式选择上的真实表现。

Abstract: Large EEG Foundation Models (FMs) have shown great potential for decoding EEG signals across diverse cognitive tasks. However, existing EEG-FM studies exhibit three critical limitations: opaque supervised baseline tuning, unverified contributions of complex learning paradigms, and a lack of transparency in model decision-making. To address these, we propose EEG-FM-Audit, a comprehensive evaluation and analysis pipeline designed to systematize the assessment of EEG-FMs. EEG-FM-Audit consists of three primary components: (1) an ASHA-driven benchmarking protocol that ensures fair comparisons by transparently optimizing supervised baselines; (2) paradigm-level ablation studies to evaluate the effectiveness of learning paradigms in FMs; and (3) a neurophysiological probing (NPP) framework, which explores whether FMs leverage valid temporal, spatial, and spectral EEG properties. We apply EEG-FM-Audit to four state-of-the-art EEG-FMs and five representative supervised models across three public datasets. Our results reveal that properly tuned supervised baselines can match or outperform advanced FMs, despite requiring significantly fewer parameters. Furthermore, we find that the effectiveness of learning paradigms of FMs is highly dependent on dataset scale and architecture. Finally, NPP analysis demonstrates how FMs rely on specific physiological features, establishing a framework for more interpretable neural decoding.

### [175] [Agile Online Model Selection: Resolving Adaptation Lag via Safeguarded Large Learning Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26919)
*Kei Takemura,Ryuta Matsuno,Keita Sakuma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决在线学习在非平稳环境中适应滞后的问题，本文提出了一种基于事后惩罚机制的大学习率优化方法，在维持理论鲁棒性的同时，大幅提升了对环境突变的响应速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平稳环境中，现有的无调参在线学习算法为了确保动态遗憾界，往往被迫限制学习率为较小的常数（如 $O(1)$），这导致了算法在面对环境突变时存在显著的适应滞后（adaptation lag）。研究旨在克服这一局限，在保证理论性能的同时提升算法的适应速度。

Method: 提出了一种新型的“乐观在线镜像下降法”（Optimistic Online Mirror Descent），其核心在于引入了一种事后惩罚机制（post-hoc penalty mechanism）。该机制能够动态监控不稳定的更新，排除掉导致过高遗憾（regret）的学习率，从而允许在算法中使用高达 $Θ(T)$ 的大学习率。

Result: 理论分析表明，该算法的累积惩罚保持在 $O(\log T)$，能够达到近乎最优的最坏情况保证，并在良性情况下表现优异。实验结果显示，该方法将环境突变后的适应滞后从数百轮缩短至少数几轮，在合成数据集和11个真实世界数据集上均显著优于现有的无调参基准方法。

Conclusion: 本研究通过事后惩罚机制成功打破了传统无调参在线学习算法在鲁棒性与灵活性之间的权衡，证明了在无需先验约束的情况下，通过大学习率优化可以实现快速的动态适应，且在理论和实践上均优于现有基准算法。

Abstract: Maintaining predictive accuracy in non-stationary environments requires online model selection to adapt autonomously to unknown distribution shifts. However, existing tuning-free algorithms face a fundamental trade-off between robustness and agility. Specifically, to ensure dynamic regret bounds, they must restrict learning rates to small constants (e.g., $O(1)$). This restriction inevitably causes significant adaptation lag during abrupt changes. To resolve this, we propose a novel optimistic online mirror descent that utilizes safeguarded large learning rates up to $Θ(T)$, where $T$ is the number of rounds. Our key technical contribution is a post-hoc penalty mechanism that dynamically monitors unstable updates and excludes learning rates incurring excessive regret, eliminating the need for restrictive a priori constraints. We show that the cumulative penalty remains $O(\log T)$, allowing our algorithm to match near-optimal worst-case guarantees while achieving superior rates in benign cases. Empirical evaluations on synthetic and eleven diverse real-world datasets demonstrate that our approach reduces the adaptation lag from hundreds of rounds to a few rounds, consistently outperforming tuning-free baselines.

</details>


### [176] [When Muon Optimizer Meets Adversarial Training: A Theoretical and Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26929)
*Jun Yan,Weiquan Huang,Jiankai Zuo,Yujian Mo,Xi Fang,Chengliang Wu,Zeming Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了使用正交化优化器（Muon）进行对抗训练的可行性。研究发现，通过正交化矩阵更新限制权重的谱增长，Muon优化器在多种架构和威胁模型下能显著优于AdamW，并与SGD表现相当，证明了优化器设计对于增强对抗鲁棒性的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对抗训练（AT）的鲁棒性高度依赖于极小极大目标的优化过程。传统的随机梯度下降（SGD）是对抗训练的默认选择，但自适应优化器（如AdamW）在标准训练中表现优异却常在对抗训练中表现不佳。Muon优化器在保持与SGD相当的内存成本前提下，在常规大模型训练中取得了成功，作者旨在探究这种正交化优化策略能否提升对抗训练在强异构威胁模型下的鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 理论分析：研究了Muon优化器通过近似极分解对矩阵更新进行正交化的机制，并证明其对矩阵更新施加了谱范数稳定性上限。2. 实证评估：在多种架构（5种）和多种威胁模型（L_inf, L_1, L_2及其联合）下，对比了Muon、SGD和AdamW在对抗训练中的表现。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了Muon优化器能限制训练过程中权重的谱增长，从而实现训练动态的稳定性。2. 实证结果显示，在CNN上Muon与SGD表现相当，但在CNN和ViT上均显著优于AdamW。3. 确认了优化器几何结构是影响对抗训练安全性的关键变量。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了优化器几何形状是对抗训练中的关键安全因素。研究表明，利用正交化更新（如Muon优化器）可以有效限制训练动态中权重的无限制谱增长，从而在无需显式权重衰减的情况下提高模型的鲁棒性。该发现为对抗训练中优化器的设计提供了新的理论指导和实证依据。

Abstract: Adversarial training (AT) remains one of the most reliable empirical defenses against adversarial attacks. Its robustness critically depends on how the underlying min-max objective is optimized. In practice, Stochastic Gradient Descent (SGD) optimizer remains the default optimization choice for AT, whereas adaptive optimizers often improve standard training but may yield inferior robustness. Recently, the Muon optimizer, which orthogonalizes matrix-valued updates via an approximate polar decomposition, has achieved notable success in large-scale training at a memory cost comparable to SGD. This raises a security-relevant question: \textit{can orthogonalized optimization improve AT under strong and heterogeneous threat models?} Focusing on this problem, we conduct a comprehensive theoretical and empirical study. Theoretically, we show that Muon imposes a spectral-norm stability ceiling on matrix updates, limiting uncontrolled spectral growth in the training dynamics without explicitly shrinking the learned weights. Empirically, across five architectures and three $\ell_p$ threat models ($\ell_\infty$, $\ell_1$, $\ell_2$) and their union, Muon is competitive with SGD on CNNs and substantially outperforms AdamW on both CNNs and ViTs. These results identify optimizer geometry as a security-relevant factor in adversarial training, while clarifying the empirical regimes in which orthogonalized updates are beneficial. Overall, our findings highlight optimizer design as a security-critical component of AT.

### [177] [RLVR Datasets and Where to Find Them: Tracing Data Lineage for Better Training Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26971)
*Hsiu-Yuan Huang,Weijie Liu,Chenming Tang,Sanwoo Lee,Kai Yang,Yangkun Chen,Saiyong Yang,Yunfang Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对RLVR领域数据溯源混乱及质量参差不齐的问题，本文提出了ATLAS追踪框架与SCA评价体系，成功去除了数据冗余与污染，构建了高质量数据集DAPO++，并验证了其在提升大模型对齐性能方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前RLVR（基于可验证奖励的强化学习）数据集生态系统碎片化，存在严重的“溯源崩溃”（provenance collapse）问题，即数据来源不清、大量重复且存在数据污染风险，这制约了模型训练的效率和公平性评估。

Method: 1. 提出了ATLAS（基于谱系感知搜索的原子源追踪）框架，将145万条数据回溯至20个原子源；2. 提出了SCA（源级反事实归因）原则，通过对比原子源检查点与基础模型，衡量样本的边际效用；3. 构建了数据集质量评分指标Q；4. 基于上述方法策划了去污染的DAPO++数据集。

Result: 1. 成功将99.7%的现有RLVR数据追溯至20个原始源；2. 实验表明大部分现有数据集缺乏创新，存在严重污染；3. 基于Qwen3系列的实验验证了DAPO++在保持性能的同时提升了训练效率，且质量指标Q能有效预测模型在下游任务中的表现。

Conclusion: 通过ATLAS框架揭示了当前RLVR数据集普遍存在的数据溯源不清和重复问题。DAPO++数据集的构建和SCA指标的提出，为评估和优化RLVR训练数据的质量提供了科学的评估标准，证明了数据纯度和溯源对于强化学习对齐性能的重要性。

Abstract: The proliferation of Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) datasets has exacerbated provenance collapse due to unclear lineage among existing datasets. To bridge this fragmented RLVR data landscape, we propose Atomic-source Tracing via Lineage-Aware Search (ATLAS), a systematic framework for tracing RLVR datasets back to their atomic sources, attributing over 99.7% of 1.45M instances to 20 atomic sources. Our analysis reveals that most RLVR datasets are variants of a small set of shared upstream sources, with few introducing genuinely new data, and many facing data contamination risks. These findings naturally motivate us to curate a new RLVR dataset, DAPO++, and to benchmark existing datasets from a lineage-aware perspective. To this end, we propose Source-level Counterfactual Attribution (SCA) as a guiding principle to curate a decontaminated training dataset with concentrated learning signals. Essentially, SCA measures a sample's marginal utility by comparing per-atomic-source RL checkpoints against a shared base model. Building upon these attribution signals, we further design a composite dataset quality score Q that strongly correlates with downstream RLVR performance. Experiments on Qwen3 series models verify that DAPO++ consistently improves performance on held-out benchmarks, while Q reliably predicts downstream RLVR training effectiveness. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/Celine-hxy/ATLAS.

### [178] [Convergence of Spectral Descent for Non-smooth Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26977)
*Yixuan Yang,Yuqing He,Song Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入探讨了Muon优化器在非光滑优化背景下的收敛特性，通过理论证明了简化版谱下降法（SD/TSD）的收敛性，并将其成功应用于鲁棒低秩矩阵恢复，填补了Muon算法在非光滑设定下理论研究的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon优化器在大语言模型训练中表现优异，但其收敛性理论目前主要依赖于平滑性假设，对于更具挑战性的非光滑优化场景，其收敛机制尚不明确，缺乏坚实的理论支撑。

Method: 研究了Muon的简化变体——谱下降法（SD）及其截断版本（TSD）。通过凸性、Lipschitz连续性和尖锐性（sharpness）假设，推导了SD和TSD在非光滑凸优化下的全局线性收敛性；并利用其与Frank-Wolfe方法的联系，推导了带权重衰减的正则化变体的次线性收敛性。此外，通过鲁棒低秩矩阵恢复问题验证了理论框架。

Result: 在非光滑凸优化设定下，证明了SD和TSD具有全局线性收敛速度；在引入正则化后，得出了次线性收敛保证；成功应用于混合噪声环境下的鲁棒低秩矩阵恢复，并提供了严谨的恢复保证；数值实验进一步验证了理论分析的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文建立了Muon类优化器在非光滑优化设定下的理论基础，证明了该类算法在凸函数优化中的收敛性，并验证了其在低秩矩阵恢复等任务中的稳健性与高效性，为理解大规模语言模型训练中的优化机制提供了重要视角。

Abstract: The Muon optimizer has recently demonstrated remarkable empirical success in training large language models. However, the theoretical understanding of its mechanisms remains limited. Current convergence guarantees for Muon rely heavily on smoothness assumptions, leaving its non-smooth convergence behavior largely unexplored. In this work, we take a step toward bridging this gap by investigating Spectral Descent (SD), a simplified variant of Muon, together with its truncated counterpart, Truncated Spectral Descent (TSD). Under convexity, Lipschitz continuity, and sharpness conditions, we establish global linear convergence for both SD and TSD in non-smooth convex formulations. We also study regularized variants equipped with decoupled weight decay and derive sublinear convergence guarantees through their connection with Frank-Wolfe methods. Finally, we apply our theoretical framework to robust low-rank matrix recovery under mixed sparse and dense noise regimes and provide rigorous recovery guarantees. Numerical experiments support the theoretical findings and demonstrate the effectiveness of Muon-type methods for non-smooth optimization.

### [179] [Sampling Data with Chains of Forward-Backward Diffusion Steps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27006)
*Hyunmo Kang,Noam Itzhak Levi,Corinna Elena Wegner,Daniel J. Korchinski,Matthieu Wyart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“U-turn链”采样方法，揭示了扩散模型在采样过程中的遍历性破缺现象及其与数据流形几何结构的联系，指出高层语义特征的生成受到局部动力学约束的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维分布采样中，利用扩散模型进行有效采样的计算效率和混合能力是一个核心挑战。论文旨在揭示扩散模型在数据流形上的局部采样动力学机制，特别是探究数据流形的碎片化如何导致遍历性破缺，以及这种动力学特性如何影响不同层级特征的生成与弛豫过程。

Method: 引入了一种基于扩散模型前向-后向短步迭代的马尔可夫链算法——“U-turn链”（U-turn chains）。该方法结合了Metropolis-Hastings修正，用于从能量修正后的目标分布中进行采样。通过分析不同U-turn幅度的动力学行为，探讨了系统在数据流形上的遍历性（ergodicity）及特征弛豫层级排序。

Result: 研究发现，极小U-turn动力学存在受数据流形碎片化驱动的遍历性破缺相变。在非遍历状态下，低层特征的弛豫速度快于高层特征；只有当U-turn幅度足够大时，遍历性才能恢复，且特征弛豫的顺序会发生反转。在自然语言和自然图像的实验中证实了这些预测，表明扩散模型采样存在明显的局部强约束与弱混合特性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，扩散模型的局部采样动力学（如U-turn链）在处理高维复杂分布（如自然语言和图像）时，受限于数据流形的局部几何约束。在大规模采样中，实现高效混合（mixing）通常需要跨越特定的相变阈值，否则系统会出现遍历性破缺，导致高层语义特征的弛豫速度明显慢于低层特征，这对基于扩散模型的采样策略设计具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Sampling from learned high-dimensional distributions is a foundational computational problem. We introduce U-turn chains: Markov chains obtained by iterating short forward-backward steps of a diffusion model, in which each step proposes a move that remains on the learned data manifold and, paired with a Metropolis-Hastings correction, samples from energy-modified targets. For synthetic languages, we show that minimal U-turn dynamics undergoes an ergodicity-breaking phase transition driven by fragmentation of the data manifold; ergodicity is restored at larger U-turn magnitude. In the non-ergodic regime, low-level features relax faster than high-level ones, an ordering that inverts only at sufficiently large U-turn magnitude. We test these predictions on natural language and natural images. In both modalities, minimal U-turns relax slowly, especially for high-level features approximated by deep representations in CNNs or LLMs. The layer-ordering inversion appears only at large noise when mixing is efficient -- signatures consistent with strongly constrained, weakly mixing local dynamics. We discuss the implications of these results for sampling with diffusion models.

</details>


### [180] [SCENT: Aligning Mass Spectra with Molecular Structure for Olfactory Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27009)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为SCENT（Spectrum-to-Chemical Embedding alignmeNT）的多模态对比学习框架。该方法通过将EI-MS生成的碎片指纹特征与预训练的分子结构嵌入（chemical structure embeddings）进行对齐，训练出一个能够仅依靠质谱数据进行嗅觉感知预测的模型。

Conclusion: SCENT框架证明了利用多模态对比学习，可以将电子电离质谱（EI-MS）这一直接获取的实验数据与人类嗅觉感知联系起来。该方法无需在推理阶段获取明确的分子结构信息，即可实现与基于结构模型相当的预测性能，为嗅觉感知预测在实际传感场景中的应用提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Predicting human olfactory perception from molecular structure has seen remarkable progress, yet these approaches require explicit chemical structure at inference, which is not available in practical sensing settings. We address this gap by exploring direct electron ionization mass spectrometry (EI-MS), a sensing technique that acquires chemically informative fragmentation fingerprints in seconds, as an alternative input modality for olfactory prediction. We contribute Spectrum-to-Chemical Embedding alignmeNT (SCENT), a multi-modal contrastive learning framework that aligns EI-MS representations with pretrained chemical structure embeddings, while requiring only mass spectra at inference. On the multi-label odor descriptor prediction task, SCENT significantly outperforms MS-only baselines and achieves performance comparable to structure-based models, despite requiring no explicit molecular structure at test time. The learned representations also better approximate continuous human perceptual ratings and generalize to real-world lab-measured spectra, suggesting that cross-modal alignment is an effective strategy for grounding analytical spectra in chemical semantics.

### [181] [SQARL: A Size-Agnostic Reinforcement Learning approach for Circuit Allocation in Distributed Quantum Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27027)
*Víctor Carballo,Júlia López-Closa,Mario Martin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Transformer的深度学习模型用于解决分布式量子计算中的“量子位分配问题”。该模型无需针对硬件拓扑进行重训，在灵活性和性能上均优于现有的强化学习方法，且在多个测试场景中超越了当前最先进的启发式算法HQA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的分布式量子计算面临量子比特扩展的限制，量子位分配问题是其中的关键挑战。现有的启发式算法（如HQA）虽然性能领先，但难以进一步优化；而现有的强化学习方案在面对不同的硬件配置时缺乏灵活性，且难以达到启发式算法的性能水平。本研究旨在通过深度学习探索更高效、更具通用性的分配策略。

Method: 提出了一种基于Transformer的深度学习架构来解决量子位分配（Qubit Allocation）问题。该模型能够处理任意数量的量子位和量子核，无需针对不同的硬件拓扑结构进行重新训练，从而克服了传统强化学习方法灵活性差的缺点，并旨在超越人工设计的启发式算法。

Result: 实验结果表明，该模型在分配成本上一致性地优于现有的强化学习方法。在Cuccaro加法器电路中，该方法相比HQA算法降低了33%的分配成本，在随机电路中平均降低了25%的成本，成功缩小了学习型算法与启发式算法之间的性能差距。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于Transformer的深度学习方法在量子位分配问题上具有巨大的潜力。通过克服传统强化学习方法在灵活性和性能上的局限性，该模型不仅在处理大规模、多架构量子处理器时表现出更好的适应性，而且在特定量子电路（如Cuccaro加法器）和随机电路中实现了对现有启发式算法（如HQA）的超越，为学习型算法在实际量子计算场景中的应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: The scaling of quantum processors is currently limited by technical challenges such as decoherence and cross-talk. As the number of qubits grows, interference increases the computational noise. Distributed quantum computing addresses these limitations by interconnecting smaller, easier-to-handle quantum processors (cores), but it introduces the challenge of minimizing slow, error-prone inter-core communication. The task of distributing quantum circuits across cores while minimizing communication costs is known as the Qubit Allocation problem. This work focuses on developing a deep learning approach to this problem, emphasizing flexibility to quantum hardware topology and improving state-of-the-art performance.
  Heuristic and non-learning algorithms, such as the Hungarian Qubit Allocation (HQA), currently represent the state of the art. Reinforcement Learning (RL) approaches leverage learned allocation policies but often lack flexibility, requiring retraining when hardware configurations change, and they fall short of the solution quality achieved by non-learning methods. However, learning mechanisms could outperform human-crafted heuristics.
  To overcome these limitations, this work proposes a flexible, transformer-based architecture that can handle arbitrary numbers of qubits and cores without retraining. Results show that the trained policy consistently outperforms the previous RL state of the art and narrows the gap between RL and HQA for the most common circuits. It achieves a 33% reduction in allocation cost relative to the HQA for the Cuccaro Adder and 25% on average for random circuits. These findings show that learning-based approaches can effectively match the performance of hand-crafted heuristics, a crucial step towards their application in real-world scenarios.

### [182] [Less is More: Early Stopping Rollout for On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27028)
*Zhou Ziheng,Jiaqi Li,Huacong Tang,Ying Nian Wu,Demetri Terzopoulos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决策略蒸馏中因离线轨迹导致的教师评估失效问题（即离线教师衰减），本文提出“提前停止采样”（ESR）方法。该方法通过限制采样长度，显著提升了模型训练的效率、稳定性和最终性能，且该机制不能简单归结为KL散度或熵值的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的策略蒸馏（On-policy Distillation）范式存在“离线教师衰减”（Off-policy Teacher Decay）问题：当学生模型生成的后续Token与其早期轨迹偏离教师分布时，教师模型对后续Token的评估能力会退化，甚至退化为预训练阶段的Token补全行为。这导致长序列生成的对齐效果不佳。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“提前停止采样”（Early Stopping Rollout, ESR）的蒸馏策略。该方法不再对学生模型进行完整序列的采样，而是将采样范围显式限制在响应的前几个Token。通过这种方式，避免了学生模型在生成长序列时因偏离教师分布而导致的评估失效问题。此外，研究还通过实验对比了ESR与传统完整序列蒸馏的性能差异，并深入分析了其背后的“级联对齐”和“子模式承诺”效应。

Result: 实验表明，ESR策略在不同模型规模、模型族、任务类型和训练配置下均优于传统的全长序列蒸馏方法。此外，ESR在GPU效率和训练稳定性方面表现更优，尤其在跨模型族场景中优势显著。分析发现，ESR通过“级联对齐”和“子模式承诺”机制，能够产生比直接模仿教师模型更好的对齐效果。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“提前停止采样”（ESR）策略通过限制采样长度，有效解决了策略蒸馏中的“离线教师衰减”问题，不仅提升了模型性能和训练稳定性，还展示了超越教师模型的潜力，为高效的大语言模型对齐提供了新路径。

Abstract: On-policy distillation has recently emerged as a promising alternative to standard sequence-level imitation, training a student by scoring its own rollouts with a teacher model. However, we observe ``Off-policy Teacher Decay'' problem in this paradigm: for the later tokens, with student's earlier trajectory as context that is off-policy to the teacher, the teacher's ability to produce a corrective score would decay, and may fall back to token-completion behavior learned in the pre-training stage. We empirically verify this problem, and we propose Early Stopping Rollout (ESR) to fix it: a simple yet effective distillation strategy that simply restricts the rollout generation to the first
  response tokens. We show that ESR both surpasses the full rollout OPD performance across model size, family, tasks and training regime, and exhibit much higher GPU efficiency and training stability, especially under cross model family scenarios. We further investigate the mechanism behind this surprising performance and discovered "Cascading Alignment" and "Sub-mode Commitment" effect of ESR that may explain why it works effectively and even sometimes exceeding the teacher model performance. Besides, we show that this position-based token selection strategy cannot be fully explainable by KL divergence and entropy signals.

</details>


### [183] [Learning Dynamic Graph Representations through Timespan View Contrasts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27063)
*Yiming Xu,Zhen Peng,Bin Shi,Xu Hua,Bo Dong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该文针对动态图的演化建模问题，提出了基于“时序平移不变性”的对比学习框架（CLDG及增强版CLDG++），通过多尺度对比学习有效捕捉图的动态特性，并在提高性能的同时显著优化了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无监督图表示学习研究主要依赖静态图的节点特征和拓扑结构，忽视了真实世界图数据中重要的时间维度信息（如边的时间戳），导致模型难以捕捉图的动态演化过程。

Method: 1. 提出“时序平移不变性”归纳偏置，假设同一节点在不同时间跨度下保持相似的标签分布；2. 构建CLDG框架，通过不同时间跨度的对比学习来维持节点的时序一致性；3. 进一步提出CLDG++，引入图扩散（graph diffusion）捕捉全局上下文相关性，并设计了局部-局部、局部-全局及全局-全局的多尺度对比学习目标。

Result: 实验结果表明，CLDG和CLDG++在节点分类和动态图异常检测任务中均取得了优异的性能；同时，由于隐式利用了时间线索而非依赖复杂的序列模型，该方法显著降低了时间和空间复杂度。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种利用时序平移不变性（temporal translation invariance）的动态图表示学习框架，有效解决了现有方法忽略图数据时间维度信息的缺陷。通过对比学习，该模型不仅在节点分类任务中表现出色，还能无缝应用于动态图异常检测，且在计算效率上优于传统的序列模型。

Abstract: The rich information underlying graphs has inspired further investigation of unsupervised graph representation. Existing studies mainly depend on node features and topological properties within static graphs to create self-supervised signals, neglecting the temporal components carried by real-world graph data, such as timestamps of edges. To overcome this limitation, this paper explores how to model temporal evolution on dynamic graphs elegantly. Specifically, we introduce a new inductive bias, namely temporal translation invariance, which illustrates the tendency of the identical node to keep similar labels across different timespans. Based on this assumption, we develop a dynamic graph representation framework CLDG that encourages the node to maintain locally consistent temporal translation invariance through contrastive learning on different timespans. Except for standard CLDG which only considers explicit topological links, our further proposed CLDG++ additionally employs graph diffusion to uncover global contextual correlations between nodes, and designs a multi-scale contrastive learning objective composed of local-local, local-global, and global-global contrasts to enhance representation capabilities. Interestingly, by measuring the consistency between different timespans to shape anomaly indicators, CLDG and CLDG++ are seamlessly integrated with the task of spotting anomalies on dynamic graphs, which has broad applications in many high-impact domains, such as finance, cybersecurity, and healthcare. Experiments demonstrate that CLDG and CLDG++ both exhibit desirable performance in downstream tasks including node classification and dynamic graph anomaly detection. Moreover, CLDG significantly reduces time and space complexity by implicitly exploiting temporal cues instead of complicated sequence models.

### [184] [Trust Region Q Adjoint Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27079)
*Yonghoon Dong,Kyungmin Lee,Changyeon Kim,Jaehyuk Kim,Jinwoo Shin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了TRQAM算法，通过在路径空间实施自适应信赖域约束来微调预训练流策略，解决了离线RL中评论家引导优化不稳定的难题，并在多项基准测试中取得了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线强化学习中，基于评论家（Critic）引导的策略优化容易因评论家估计误差的放大而导致模型崩溃。现有的QAM方法虽有所改进，但在评论家条件不好时仍不稳定。因此，需要一种能够更稳定地微调预训练流策略的算法。

Method: 作者提出了“信任域Q-伴随匹配”（TRQAM）算法。该方法将问题重构为具有约束的随机最优控制（SOC）问题，通过投影对偶下降自适应地调节信赖域参数λ，并推导出了路径空间KL散度与λ之间的闭式解，从而实现对策略偏离预训练模型的精确控制。

Result: 在50个OGBench任务的测试中，TRQAM在离线强化学习和离线转在线强化学习任务上均优于现有最优方法。特别是在离线强化学习任务中，其成功率达到了68%，显著超过了此前最优基准的46%。

Conclusion: 本文提出的TRQAM算法通过在路径空间引入信赖域约束，有效解决了离线强化学习中因评论家误差导致的优化不稳定问题，为预训练流策略的微调提供了一种稳健且高效的新范式。

Abstract: Off-policy reinforcement learning of pretrained flow policies remains challenging due to the instability of optimization arising from the multi-step sampling process. Recently, Q-learning with Adjoint Matching (QAM) addressed this issue by reformulating into a memoryless stochastic optimal control (SOC) problem with a learned critic. However, QAM inherits a fundamental fragility of critic-guided improvement: small critic errors are amplified when critics are ill-conditioned, often leading to model collapse. This paper introduces Trust Region Q-Adjoint Matching (TRQAM), a stable off-policy fine-tuning algorithm that adaptively controls the path-space KL with pretrained flow policies through projected dual descent. Specifically, we optimize the trust-region parameter $λ$ in SOC dynamics, and theoretically show that the path-space KL can be represented by a closed-form function of $λ$. As a result, our method can precisely control the exact deviation from pretrained flow policies, achieving stable off-policy RL. Through experiments on 50 OGBench tasks, TRQAM consistently outperforms prior arts in both offline RL and offline-to-online RL. In particular, TRQAM achieves an overall success rate of 68% in offline RL, substantially improves the strongest baseline at 46%.

### [185] [ReMoE: Boosting Expert Reuse through Router Fine-Tuning in Memory-Constrained MoE LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27081)
*Xiongwei Zhu,Xiaojian Liao,Tianyang Jiang,Yusen Zhang,Liang Wang,Limin Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ReMoE 是一种优化 MoE 模型推理的路由微调框架，通过引导模型选择最近使用的专家，显著提升了专家缓存命中率，有效解决了内存受限场景下的 I/O 瓶颈，大幅提升了推理吞吐速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模细粒度 MoE 模型推理中，受限于硬件内存，无法一次性加载所有专家。若频繁从慢速外部存储加载未缓存的专家，会导致严重的 I/O 阻塞，限制推理吞吐量。因此，迫切需要一种方法来提高专家使用的局部性，以减少缓存未命中。

Method: 提出 ReMoE 框架，通过微调 MoE 模型的路由层（Router），引入偏置机制，使得模型倾向于在短时间内重复利用最近激活的专家。这种方法通过增加专家使用的时间局部性（Temporal Locality），从而更好地契合缓存约束，减少从外部存储读取专家参数的频率，且不增加额外的推理计算开销。

Result: 在 DeepSeek 和 Qwen 模型上的实验表明，ReMoE 在保证下游任务性能的前提下，将专家重用率提高了 26%。在 vLLM（GPU-CPU 卸载）环境下，吞吐量提升了 8.4%；在 Jetson Orin NX 平台的 llama.cpp 环境下，首字延迟（TPOT）降低了 43.6%-49.8%，解码速度提升了 1.77-1.99 倍。

Conclusion: ReMoE 提出了一种通过微调路由策略以增强专家时间局部性的有效方法，证明了在内存受限的场景下，通过软件层面的算法优化能够显著缓解 I/O 瓶颈，从而提升 MoE 模型在边缘设备和卸载推理环境下的实际部署性能。

Abstract: Fine-grained Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models sparsely activate only a subset of experts per token, reducing activated computation while maintaining high model capacity. However, in memory-constrained inference scenarios, only a small set of experts can be cached. Experts not in the cache must be fetched from slow external storage (e.g., UFS), leading to frequent evictions and substantial I/O overhead.
  We propose ReMoE, a router fine-tuning framework designed to boost token-wise expert reuse. ReMoE biases the router toward recently selected experts, producing temporally stable routing that better matches cache locality constraints. By increasing short-horizon expert reuse, ReMoE reduces expert fetches from storage without adding inference-time computation.
  Experiments on DeepSeek and Qwen models show that ReMoE improves expert reuse by 26% while maintaining downstream task performance. Real-system evaluations further confirm these benefits, improving output throughput by 8.4% under vLLM GPU-CPU expert offloading and reducing TPOT by 43.6-49.8% under llama.cpp on Jetson Orin NX, corresponding to a 1.77-1.99$\times$ decode speedup across diverse workloads. Checkpoints and usage instructions are available at https://github.com/BUAA-OSCAR/ReMoE.

</details>


### [186] [Adversarial Dual On-Policy Distillation from Expressive Flow-based Teacher](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27095)
*Zhenglin Wan,Jingxuan Wu,Xingrui Yu,Chubin Zhang,Mingcong Lei,Bo An,Ivor W. Tsang,Yang You*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FA-OPD 是一种新型的从演示学习方法，通过协同训练流匹配教师和学生模型，解决了传统行为克隆方法在未见状态下表现不佳的问题，在多种机器人控制任务中实现了更稳健的在线学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的行为克隆方法（包括基于扩散或流匹配的策略）多为离线监督学习，训练时无法获取策略实际访问状态下的修正信号，导致严重的分布偏移（Distributional Shift）问题。此外，标准的在线蒸馏（OPD）方法依赖于固定的专家策略，而在仅有演示数据的场景下无法直接应用。

Method: 提出了一种名为“对抗性双重在线蒸馏”（FA-OPD）的方法。该方法核心在于联合训练一个流匹配（Flow Matching）教师模型和一个轻量级 MLP 学生模型。教师通过两个渠道反馈信息：一是通过奖励渠道学习专家相似度，指导策略进行长视野在线探索；二是通过动作渠道提供局部动作目标，稳定策略的学习过程。两者相互耦合，实现了探索与利用的平衡。

Result: 在六个涵盖机器人导航、操作和运动的任务基准测试中，FA-OPD 表现出超越现有强基准方法的性能，并且在演示数据有限或存在噪声的情况下具有更强的稳健性。

Conclusion: FA-OPD 通过整合生成式模型与对抗性在线蒸馏，成功克服了传统行为克隆在处理分布偏移问题上的局限，为从演示中学习具身控制策略提供了一种高效、稳健的框架，特别是在数据稀疏或带有噪声的情况下表现优异。

Abstract: Learning from demonstrations in embodied control is often cast as behavioral cloning, and recent diffusion or flow-matching policies improve this paradigm by modeling multi-modal expert actions. Yet these methods remain offline supervised learners: the policy is trained only on expert states and receives no corrective signal on the states it actually visits. On-policy distillation (OPD) offers a natural remedy, but standard OPD assumes a strong fixed teacher, which is unavailable in demonstration-only control. We propose \textbf{FA-OPD}, an \emph{adversarial dual on-policy distillation} method in which a Flow Matching (FM) teacher is learned from demonstrations and co-trained with a lightweight MLP student. The teacher provides two complementary signals on student rollouts. The reward channel learns an expert-likeness objective over state-action pairs and drives online exploration through long-horizon policy optimization. The action channel supplies dense local targets at student-visited states, stabilizing exploitation. FA-OPD couples them so that reward distillation enables generalization beyond point-wise demonstrations, while action distillation keeps exploration anchored near expert-like behavior. Across six robot navigation, manipulation, and locomotion benchmarks, FA-OPD beats strong baselines and shows much stronger robustness under noisy or limited demonstrations.

### [187] [DEI: Diversity in Evolutionary Inference for Quality-Diversity Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27130)
*John Donaghy,Shikhar Rastogi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种分布式质量-多样性（QD）搜索框架DEI，通过利用异构LLM的差异化先验作为互补的演化突变算子，显著提升了搜索的质量与覆盖率，证明了模型多样性在演化推理中的核心价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的同构并行搜索方法会导致模型偏差（Inductive Biases）在所有工作节点中被复制，从而限制了探索的多样性。研究旨在通过利用不同LLM独特的创造性先验，将其作为行为新颖性的互补来源，从而打破单一模型在演化搜索中的局限性。

Method: 提出了DEI（演化推理中的多样性）框架。该框架采用分布式QD搜索，将异构的大语言模型（LLMs）作为突变算子分配到对等节点上，并通过非阻塞集体操作进行通信。各节点在每轮结束后共享局部最优解，通过“数字红皇后”机制形成跨模型对抗压力。

Result: 在Core War领域中，由四种异构LLM组成的集成框架在相同总调用预算下，QD得分比单节点基线高出124%，覆盖率高出28%；同时在QD得分、覆盖率及解决方案通用性上均显著优于同构集成方案。

Abstract: We present DEI: Diversity in Evolutionary Inference, a distributed Quality-Diversity (QD) search framework that assigns heterogeneous large language models (LLMs) as mutation operators across peer nodes communicating with non-blocking collective operations. Unlike homogeneous parallel search, which replicates a single model's inductive biases across all workers, DEI treats each LLM's distinct creative prior as a complementary source of behavioral novelty. Extending the Digital Red Queen framework with DEI, nodes share local optimal solutions at the end of each round to seed the next round's population. This creates cross-model adversarial pressure that drives robustness beyond intra-model self-play. Evaluated on the Core War domain, a competitive programming benchmark in which Redcode warrior programs battle inside a simulated machine, a four-node heterogeneous ensemble (GPT-5.4-mini, Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.2, and Claude Haiku 4.5) achieves 124 percent higher merged-archive QD-Score (45.90 vs. 20.46) and 28 percent higher coverage (80.6 percent vs. 63.0 percent of cells) than a single-node baseline at equal total LLM-call budget. The heterogeneous ensemble also outperforms an equally-budgeted homogeneous ensemble on QD-Score, coverage, and held-out solution generality across all four model families. These results provide the first empirical evidence that model diversity, not merely parallelism, is the key driver of gain in distributed LLM-based QD search.
